# Context Mode Index

Index local project content for later search.

## Instructions

1. Prefer the `ctx_index` MCP tool when it is available.
2. Ask for a path only if the user did not provide one and the current project root is ambiguous.
3. Use `path`, not large inline `content`, so file bytes do not enter the conversation.
4. For repository indexing, pass conservative bounds and a clear source label:

```javascript
ctx_index({
  path: ".",
  source: "project:<name>",
  maxDepth: 5,
  maxFiles: 200
})
```

5. If MCP tools are unavailable, fall back to the CLI:

```bash
context-mode index . --source project:<name>
```

6. Report the indexed source label, file count or section count, and the matching search command:

```javascript
ctx_search({ source: "project:<name>", queries: ["..."] })
```

## Safety

- Do not index dependency directories, build outputs, secrets, or generated artifacts.
- Prefer `--exclude` or `exclude` for project-specific noisy paths.
- For broad repos, ask the user before raising `maxFiles` above 500.

1	# Problems discovered while designing/implementing the test suite
2	
3	Logged during the 2026-07-04 test-suite work (see `PROMPT.md` / `SPEC.md` in this folder). Per
4	the driving prompt, program bugs are **logged here and fixed in a later session**. P1 below was
5	originally believed to be a blocking bug; during implementation it was **disproven** (see its
6	corrected entry). P9/P10 were found while *running* the code during implementation.
7	
8	Line numbers refer to the working revision (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails`). After the Part A
9	extraction the file shifted; treat line numbers as starting points and re-locate by symptom.
10	
11	Most entries were found by **reading** the code; P9/P10 were **reproduced** during

15	---
16	
17	## P1 — NOT A BUG (disproven during implementation): the ≤4-month path already renders
18	
19	**Original claim (design time).** That a site with ≤4 months of traffic would `NameError` on
20	`median_visitors` / `site_current_plan_index` / `site_recommended_plan_index` while building
21	`template_dict`, because those are assigned only inside `if len(v) > 4:`.
22	
23	**Why it is wrong.** The design-time check missed the **earlier default initializers**:
24	- `median_visitors = 0`, `cost_same = {}`, `costs_median = {}`, `cost_table_rows = {}` are set
25	  **before** the `if len(v) > 4:` block (originally L3097–3100).
26	- `site_current_plan`, `site_recommended_plan`, `site_current_plan_index = 0`,
27	  `site_recommended_plan_index = 0` are all initialized right after plan resolution (L985–988).
28	
29	So every variable `template_dict` consumes is defined for a ≤4-month site, and the "not enough
30	data yet" state renders fine.
31	
32	**Confirmed empirically.** The offline e2e for `its-wws-test1` has only one in-window month (the
33	recorded metrics fall after the March report date), so it **already renders the ≤4-month state**
34	("needs 4 months more data", "Cost estimates will be available once the site has five months…").
35	`tests/e2e/test_recommendation_e2e.py::test_new_site_shows_not_enough_data` pins this. No code
36	fix was made (there was nothing to fix); the "fix blocking bug now" decision is moot.
37	
38	**Coverage note.** Because the offline golden only ever hits the ≤4-month state, the extracted
39	`plan_costs` cost model is exercised end-to-end by a dedicated e2e that seeds >4 in-window months
40	(`test_recommendation_e2e.py::test_recommendation_path_exercises_plan_costs`) plus the
41	`plan_costs` unit/property tests.
42	
43	---
44	
45	## P2 — Config-defined `[News]` items are never added (dead loop)
46	
47	**Symptom.** News items written inline in the config file's `[News]` table never appear in
48	reports. Only news loaded from `*.toml` files in `[News].folder` works.
49	
50	**Root cause (L863–870).**
51	```python
52	if "News" in sc.config:
53	    for news_item_name in sc.config["News"].keys():
54	        if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict):
55	            continue  # skip News configuration directives
56	        sc.add_news_item(sc.config["News"][news_item_name], ...)
57	```
58	`news_item_name` is a **dict key (a string)**, so `isinstance(news_item_name, dict)` is always
59	`False` and the `continue` always fires — the `add_news_item` call is unreachable. The guard was
60	presumably meant to test the *value* (`sc.config["News"][news_item_name]`) and skip scalar
61	directives like `folder`.
62	
63	**Fix (later).** Iterate items and skip non-table values, e.g.
64	`for name, value in sc.config["News"].items(): if not isinstance(value, dict): continue`. Confirm
65	the `folder` key (a string) is correctly skipped and only `[News.<x>]` sub-tables are added.
66	
67	**Test coverage now.** A strict-`xfail` unit/integration test documents the intended behavior
68	(config-inline news item shows up) and will flip to passing when fixed. The file-based news path
69	is tested normally.
70	
71	---
72	
73	## P3 — `terminus()` swallows `errors`/`fatal` and returns `""` on JSON-decode failure
74	
75	**Root cause (L338–353).** `terminus()` returns **only `result`** (the `return result, errors, fatal`
76	line is commented at L352). On a `json.JSONDecodeError` it sets `result = ""` (L343, self-marked
77	`# TODO: set to None`) and continues. For non-session errors it prints `Terminus error: …`
78	(L346) but neither raises, exits, nor signals the caller.
79	
80	**Consequences.**
81	- Callers index directly into the result: `terminus("plan:info", …)["sku"]` (~L972),
82	  `terminus(...)["timeseries"]` (~L490/L1081/L1095). When `result == ""`, `""["sku"]` raises
83	  `TypeError: string indices must be integers` — a crash far from the real cause (a malformed
84	  Terminus response), with the original stderr already discarded.
85	- Empty-but-valid decode (`result == {}` / `[]`) silently produces zero rows with no signal.
86	
87	**Fix (later).** Adopt the TODO: return `(result, errors, fatal)` (and `None`, not `""`, on
88	decode failure); update call sites to check `fatal` / `None`. This is entangled with the broader
89	"`terminus()` → return tuple" item already in the README TODO list.
90	
91	**Test coverage now.** Integration tests around the `run_terminus` seam pin the *current* return
92	contract (single value) and the session-expiry retry; a strict-`xfail` documents the desired
93	`(result, errors, fatal)` contract so the later change is guarded.
94	
95	---
96	
97	## P4 — DNS resolution failures are console-only and conflated with "not in DNS"
98	
99	**Root cause (L1252–1259 for A, L1282–1289 for AAAA).** `NoAnswer` / `NXDOMAIN` /
100	`NoNameservers` / `Timeout` are each caught and only `sc.console.print(...)`ed. Control then falls
101	through; `dns_points_at_cloudflare` / `dns_points_elsewhere` remain 0, so L1291 emits
102	`ATTENTION: {hostname} is not in DNS` — i.e. a **transient resolver timeout is reported
103	identically to a genuinely-unregistered hostname**, and neither becomes a structured
104	`site_context` notice (only console output). Observability gap: the report can't distinguish
105	"DNS is broken right now" from "this domain doesn't exist."
106	
107	**Fix (later).** Distinguish transient (`Timeout` / `NoNameservers`) from definitive
108	(`NXDOMAIN` / `NoAnswer`) outcomes; surface at least the definitive ones as a report notice via
109	`sc.add_notice(...)` rather than console-only.
110	
111	**Test coverage now.** Not directly tested this round (DNS is stubbed out in offline e2e via
112	`fqdns.json = {}` and platform-only `domain:list`). Logged for the later observability pass.
113	
114	---
115	
116	## P5 — `emails_sent` counter is dead; `--all` summary line is misleading
117	
118	**Root cause (L3658, L3676).** `emails_sent += 1` is commented out (SMTP send is disabled), so
119	the counter is never incremented. The only reader is L3676 `f"Email sent for {emails_sent} of
120	{site_count} sites."`, inside the `if sc.options.all:` branch.
121	
122	**Consequences.**
123	- The summary always says "Email sent for 0 of N sites" even after a successful dry run.
124	- If `emails_sent` is not initialized before the loop, L3676 would `NameError` under `--all`
125	  (needs confirmation — this path is **out of test scope** because `--all` is forbidden).
126	
127	**Fix (later, together with SMTP re-enable).** Restore the increment when send is re-enabled and
128	initialize `emails_sent = 0` before the loop; make the dry-run summary count intended-recipients
129	rather than sent.
130	
131	**Test coverage now.** None (lives behind `--all`, which is never run). Logged only.
132	
133	---
134	
135	## P6 — Stale docstring return signatures on Terminus wrappers
136	
137	**Root cause.** `wp()` (L356), `wp_eval()` (L370), and `drush()` (L427) are annotated/documented
138	as returning 2-tuples (`-> (Any, str)` / `-> (str, str)`) but actually return **3-tuples**
139	`(result, errors, fatal)`; call sites unpack three (e.g. `ocp_config, errors, fatal = wp_eval(...)`
140	~L1685). Cosmetic/maintainability, not a runtime bug, but misleads readers and future callers.
141	
142	**Fix (later).** Correct the annotations/docstrings to the real 3-tuple contract.
143	
144	**Test coverage now.** Integration `test_wrappers.py` asserts the *actual* 3-tuple shape, which
145	documents the truth regardless of the stale annotations.
146	
147	---
148	
149	## P7 — Misleading comment references a non-existent option
150	
151	**Root cause (L3666).** `plt.close(fig)  # needed to free up memory when sc.options.all_sites is
152	True`. The parsed option is `all` (`--all/-a`), not `all_sites`; `sc.options.all_sites` does not
153	exist. Comment-only; no runtime effect.
154	
155	**Fix (later).** Correct the comment to `sc.options.all`.
156	
157	---
158	
159	## P8 — Institution-specific (U-M) logic in the core script not behind `[UMich].enabled`
160	
161	**Not a bug for U-M runs**, but a **reusability defect**: for any non-U-M deployment these paths
162	either hardcode U-M specifics or risk `KeyError`. Two in-code comments (≈L3410–3411, L3494–3497)
163	already document that previous `if True:` blocks here crashed non-U-M runs with
164	`KeyError('UMich')` and were retrofitted with a guard — evidence the guarding is incomplete.
165	
166	Catalogue (re-verify lines at fix time) of U-M specifics **not** behind the
167	`"UMich" in sc.config and sc.config["UMich"]["enabled"]` guard:
168	- `smtp_login()` — hardcoded `smtp.mail.umich.edu:465` + `SMTP_PASSWORD` (L771).
169	- `umich-cloudflare` cache check + `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/5114` (L1569–1577), gated
170	  only by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) > 0`.
171	- `umich-oidc-login` reinstall special-case (semver, GitHub release URLs, U-M shortcode text)
172	  inside the generic plugins loop (L1595–1650).
173	- Drupal user-agent check → `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4242`, `ifconfig.me/ua`
174	  (L2093, L2137–2150).
175	- Support-URL notice strings `its.umich.edu/computing/web-mobile/pantheon/support`
176	  (L1014, L1024) and Cloudflare "at U-M" doc URLs (L1429–1471).
177	- `make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` — unconditional (L3533–3534).
178	- MIME headers unconditional (L3607–3617): `From: … <webmaster@umich.edu>`, dry-run `To:` /
179	  `Bcc:` `@umich.edu` / `@go.mail.umich.edu`, `Reply-to: webmaster@umich.edu`.
180	- Hardcoded site-name special cases `lsa-disko-project`, `umma-inside-wp` (L3390–3392) — inside
181	  the guard, but still string-literal site names.
182	
183	**Fix (later — this is the planned "move institution logic into plugins/config" stage).** Move
184	each behind `[UMich].enabled` and/or into the `umich` plugin/check packages, or drive from config
185	(`[Email].from`, `[Email].reply_to`, doc-URL map, `make_msgid` domain). Add non-U-M-config e2e
186	coverage once guarded.
187	
188	**Test coverage now.** Not fixed this round. The offline e2e runs *with* U-M behavior baked in
189	(the golden reflects it), so these paths are exercised but not proven reusable. A future
190	non-U-M-config golden would prove the guarding.
191	
192	---
193	
194	## P9 — Report HTML has links without discernible text (WCAG "link-name"), reproduced
195	
196	**Found by** the render tier's axe-core accessibility smoke (`tests/render/test_render.py`),
197	which flags one **serious** violation, `link-name` ("Ensure links have discernible text"), on
198	**both** the WordPress and Drupal reports. This is a real WCAG 2 A / Section 508 issue: at least
199	one anchor in `email_template.html` (and/or a runtime-injected section such as the SiteLens
200	gauges) wraps only a non-text element without an accessible name (empty/again-missing `alt`, or
201	an icon-only link).
202	
203	**Status.** Allowlisted in the render test (`_AXE_ALLOWLIST` includes `link-name`) with an
204	explicit comment, so the a11y smoke still fails on *new* serious/critical issues while
205	acknowledging this pre-existing debt. **Fix later** by giving every anchor discernible text
206	(link text or a non-empty `img alt` / `aria-label`), then remove `link-name` from the allowlist.
207	
208	**Verify at fix time.** `./run-tests -m render` passes after removing `link-name` from
209	`_AXE_ALLOWLIST`.
210	
211	---
212	
213	## P10 — `IndexError` when a site has zero traffic history
214	
215	**Symptom (reproduced).** Running the report for a site with **no** `pantheon_traffic` rows
216	crashes: `main()` does `days = sorted(plan_on_day.keys())` then `plan = plan_on_day[days[0]]`
217	(around L2678 post-refactor). With no traffic, `plan_on_day` is empty and `days[0]` raises
218	`IndexError: list index out of range`.
219	
220	**How it surfaced.** Recording Drupal fixtures against `its-wws-test2` (a fresh site with no
221	live traffic) crashed here until the recording flow was changed to **seed a month of traffic
222	before the live run** (`tests/tools/record.py`). The harness already sidesteps this in the
223	offline e2e by seeding traffic (see the `seed_traffic` note in `conftest.py`).
224	
225	**Fix later.** Guard the aggregation: if `plan_on_day` is empty, emit a notice / skip the plan
226	sections gracefully rather than indexing `days[0]`. This is the same class of "a genuinely new
227	site" robustness gap as P1's (non-)issue, but here it is a real crash.
228	
229	**Verify at fix time.** A site (or seeded DB) with zero in-window traffic renders a report (or a
230	clean "no traffic yet" message) instead of raising `IndexError`.
231	
232	---
233	
234	## Non-issues considered and dismissed
235	- `terminus()` retry list-mutation (L331–337) — previously a real crash on a `*args` tuple; the
236	  code now converts to a list first and is correct. Regression already exists in the harness.
237	- `check/umich/__init__.py` `sc.console('…')`-as-callable — already fixed; regression exists.
238

Test tiers are mark-based (`unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`) per the `markers` list in `pyproject.toml`.

## P2 — dead config-`[News]` loop — CONFIRMED

`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` lines **977-993**:

```python
    if "News" in sc.config:
        for news_item_name in sc.config["News"].keys():
            if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict):
                continue  # skip News configuration directives
            sc.add_news_item(
                sc.config["News"][news_item_name],
                f"{news_item_name} in configuration file {sc.options.config}",
            )
    for filename in sorted(glob.glob(f"{sc.config['News']['folder']}/*.toml")):
        with open(filename, "rb") as f:
            n = tomllib.load(f)
            if "News" not in n:
                sys.exit(f'News item in {filename} is missing the "News" key.')
            for news_item_name in n["News"].keys():
                sc.add_news_item(
                    n["News"][news_item_name], f"{news_item_name} in file {filename}"
                )
```

**Confirmed the `continue` always fires.** `news_item_name` is a KEY produced by `.keys()` — always a string (e.g. `"folder"`, `"support-page-improvements"`), never a `dict`. So `not isinstance(news_item_name, dict)` is always `True` and `sc.add_news_item(...)` on lines 981-984 is dead code. The check should be against the VALUE, `sc.config["News"][news_item_name]`, and it should also skip the `folder` directive key.

**Contrast — the file-based loader (lines 985-993) is correct:** it iterates `n["News"].keys()` and passes the VALUE `n["News"][news_item_name]` (a dict, the TOML subtable `[News.&lt;name&gt;]`) to `add_news_item`. The config `[News]` section in `sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` (lines 115-125) has the same shape: a scalar `folder = "./news"` directive plus `[News.&lt;name&gt;]` subtables holding `order`/`icon`/`message`. So "correct" for the config loop means: iterate the keys, skip non-dict values (the `folder` string), and pass the dict value.

**`sc.add_news_item` signature** — `/workspace/script_context.py` line **80**:

```python
def add_news_item(news_item: dict, from_where: str = 'check') -&gt; None:
```

## P3 — `terminus()` swallowing errors — CONFIRMED

`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` lines **327-353**:

```python
def terminus(*args) -&gt; Any:
    """
    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return the result as a JSON object.
    """
    # args is a tuple (from *args); work with a list so the retry sentinel can be
    # added/removed without mutating a tuple (which previously crashed this path).
    args = list(args)
    retry = True
    if "pshe-no-retry" in args:
        args.remove("pshe-no-retry")
        retry = False
    command = [*args, "--format=json"]
    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
    try:
        result = json.loads(output)
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        result = ""  # TODO: set to None
        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
    if errors != "":
        sc.console.print(f"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}")
        if retry and "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session" in errors:
            sc.console.print("Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...")
            time.sleep(5)
            args.append("pshe-no-retry")
            return terminus(*args)
    # return result, errors.strip(), fatal  # TODO
    return result
```

**Confirmed:** returns only `result` (line 353, single value); the 3-tuple return `return result, errors.strip(), fatal` is commented out (line 352); on `json.JSONDecodeError` it sets `result = ""` (line 343). Errors are only printed (line 346), not propagated to the caller. `fatal` is computed but discarded.

**Call sites that index into the return value:**
- Line **1084**: `site_plan_info = terminus("plan:info", site["name"])`, then line **1085** `if "sku" not in site_plan_info:` and line **1090** `plan_sku = site_plan_info["sku"]`. (When JSON decode fails, `result == ""`, so `"sku" not in ""` is `True` → falls into the ERROR branch and `sys.exit("Bailing out.")` at line 1089. A string index like `""["sku"]` would raise `TypeError` if reached.)
- Line **487**: `metrics = terminus("env:metrics", site_env, f"--period={period}")`, then line **490** `for e in metrics["timeseries"]:` and line **491** `entry = metrics["timeseries"][e]`.
- Line **1193**: `metrics = terminus("env:metrics", live_site, "--period=day")`, then line **1207** `for e in metrics["timeseries"]:` and line **1208** `entry = metrics["timeseries"][e]`.

Note: these assign the return to a variable first, then index it (not literally `terminus(...)["sku"]` inline), but the failure mode is identical — on a swallowed error `result == ""`, and `""["timeseries"]` / `"" in`-checks misbehave (`TypeError` on subscript).

**`run_terminus` signature and return contract** — line **237**:

```python
def run_terminus(command: list, input_data=None) -&gt; (str, str, bool):
```

It returns a 3-tuple `(output, errors, fatal)`: `output`/`errors` are the stripped decoded stdout/stderr strings, `fatal` is a bool (e.g. `return output, errors, True` on `TimeoutExpired`, line 269).

## P4 — DNS resolution failure handling — CONFIRMED

`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` lines **1341-1407**:

```python
                dns_points_at_cloudflare = 0
                dns_points_elsewhere = 0
                try:
                    a = dns.resolver.resolve(hostname, "A")
                    for rdata in a:
                        address = ipaddress.ip_address(rdata.address)
                        if cloudflare_enabled and any(
                            [
                                address in net
                                for net in sc.plugin_context["plugin.cloudflare"][
                                    "cloudflare_ipv4_nets"
                                ]
                            ]
                        ):
                            dns_points_at_cloudflare += 1
                            sc.console.print(
                                f"{hostname} has [green]Cloudflare IP address {rdata.address}[/green]"
                            )
                        else:
                            dns_points_elsewhere += 1
                            sc.console.print(
                                f"{hostname} has IP address [red]{rdata.address}[/red]"
                            )
                except dns.resolver.NoAnswer:
                    sc.console.print(f"No A record for {hostname}", style="red")
                except dns.resolver.NXDOMAIN:
                    sc.console.print(f"NXDOMAIN for {hostname} (A)", style="red")
                except dns.resolver.NoNameservers:
                    sc.console.print(f"No nameservers for {hostname}", style="red")
                except dns.resolver.Timeout:
                    sc.console.print(f"Timeout resolving {hostname}", style="red")

                try:
                    aaaa = dns.resolver.resolve(hostname, "AAAA")
                    for rdata in aaaa:
                        address = ipaddress.ip_address(rdata.address)
                        if cloudflare_enabled and any(
                            [
                                address in net
                                for net in sc.plugin_context["plugin.cloudflare"][
                                    "cloudflare_ipv6_nets"
                                ]
                            ]
                        ):
                            dns_points_at_cloudflare += 1
                            sc.console.print(
                                f"{hostname} has [green]Cloudflare IP address {rdata.address}[/green]"
                            )
                        else:
                            dns_points_elsewhere += 1
                            sc.console.print(
                                f"{hostname} has IP address [red]{rdata.address}[/red]"
                            )
                except dns.resolver.NoAnswer:
                    sc.console.print(f"No AAAA record for {hostname}")
                except dns.resolver.NXDOMAIN:
                    sc.console.print(f"NXDOMAIN for {hostname} (AAAA)", style="red")
                except dns.resolver.NoNameservers:
                    sc.console.print(f"No nameservers for {hostname}", style="red")
                except dns.resolver.Timeout:
                    sc.console.print(f"Timeout resolving {hostname}", style="red")

                if dns_points_at_cloudflare == 0 and dns_points_elsewhere == 0:
                    sc.console.print(
                        f":exclamation: [bold red] ATTENTION: {hostname} is not in DNS"
                    )
                    not_in_dns.append(hostname)
```

**Confirmed.** All four exception handlers for both the A block (1364-1371) and AAAA block (1394-1401) only call `sc.console.print(...)` — no notice/warning is added, and the counters `dns_points_at_cloudflare` / `dns_points_elsewhere` stay at 0. So a genuine DNS failure (`NoAnswer`/`NXDOMAIN`/`NoNameservers`/`Timeout`) is indistinguishable from "not in DNS": at line 1403 both counters being 0 triggers the `ATTENTION: {hostname} is not in DNS` console print (1404-1406) and appends to `not_in_dns` (line 1407) — but again only a console print, not a `sc.add_notice`. Note the AAAA `NoAnswer` handler at line 1395 is missing `style="red"` (a very common/normal case). The Cloudflare-specific attention checks follow at lines 1408-1421.

**`sc.add_notice` signature** — `/workspace/script_context.py` line **65**:

```python
def add_notice(notice: dict, site_context: dict) -&gt; None:
```

(Note: `sc.add_notice` is defined but has zero call sites in the script; notices are appended via other paths / the DNS issues above never reach it.)

## P6 — stale wrapper docstrings — CONFIRMED

`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails`:

`wp()` — lines **356-367**:

```python
def wp(siteenv: str, *args) -&gt; (Any, str):
    """
    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as JSON.
    """
    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
    try:
        result = json.loads(output)
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        result = None
        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
```

`wp_eval()` — lines **370-376**:

```python
def wp_eval(siteenv: str, *args) -&gt; (str, str):
    """
    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as a string.
    """
    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", "eval", *args]
    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
    return output.strip(), errors.strip(), fatal
```

`drush()` — lines **427-439**:

```python
def drush(siteenv: str, *args) -&gt; (Any, str):
    """
    Run a "drush" command through Terminus and return the result as a JSON object.
    """
    command = ["drush", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
    output, errors = fix_drush_output(output, errors)
    try:
        result = json.loads(output)
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        result = None
        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
```

**Confirmed:** each return annotation declares a 2-tuple (`(Any, str)`, `(str, str)`, `(Any, str)`) but every function actually returns a 3-tuple `(result/output, errors.strip(), fatal)` (lines 367, 376, 439). The `wp()` docstring is also wrong content-wise — it says "wp eval" / "return the result as JSON" but runs a generic `wp` command. (Sibling `drush_php_script()` at 442-454 has the same 2-tuple-annotation / 3-tuple-return mismatch.)

**A call site unpacking three values** — line **1648**:

```python
            plugins, errors, fatal = wp(
```

(Other 3-value unpack sites: line 1513 `network_home_url, errors, fatal = wp_eval(`, line 1624 `wordpress_version, errors, fatal = wp_eval(`, line 1797 `ocp_config, errors, fatal = wp_eval(`, line 1454 `sites_file, errors, fatal = drush_php_script(`.) So all callers rely on the 3-tuple; the 2-tuple annotations are simply stale.

## P10 — IndexError on zero traffic — CONFIRMED

`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` lines **2654-2691**:

```python
        # Create an array containing the sum of visits by month:
        visits_by_month = {}
        plan_on_day = {}
        d = start_date
        while d &lt;= end_date:
            month = d.strftime("%Y-%m")
            visits_by_month[month] = 0
            d = d.replace(day=1) + datetime.timedelta(days=32)
            d = d.replace(day=1)
        for row in results:
            month = row.traffic_date.strftime("%Y-%m")
            visits_by_month[month] += row.visits
            plan_on_day[row.traffic_date] = row.site_plan
        if sc.options.verbose:
            pprint(visits_by_month)
            if sc.options.verbose &gt; 1:
                pprint(plan_on_day)

        # Create a list of time ranges when the site was on each plan
        last_day = calendar.monthrange(end_date.year, end_date.month)[1]
        plot_right_date = end_date.replace(day=last_day)
        plan_over_time = []
        # noinspection PyTypeChecker
        days = sorted(plan_on_day.keys())
        plan = plan_on_day[days[0]]
        plan_start = days[0]
        for i in range(1, len(days)):
            today = days[i]
            if plan_on_day[today] != plan:
                plan_over_time.append(
                    {"start": plan_start, "end": days[i - 1], "plan": plan}
                )
                plan_start = today
                plan = plan_on_day[plan_start]
        plan_over_time.append(
            {"start": plan_start, "end": plot_right_date, "plan": plan}
        )
        sc.debug(plan_over_time)
```

**Confirmed the IndexError.** `plan_on_day` is initialized empty at line **2656** and is populated ONLY inside `for row in results:` (line **2666**, `plan_on_day[row.traffic_date] = row.site_plan`). `results` is the DB query at line 1270 (`db_session.query(PantheonTraffic).filter(...).all()`). If a site has zero traffic rows in the window, the loop body never runs, so `plan_on_day` stays `{}`, `days = sorted(plan_on_day.keys())` (line **2677**) is `[]`, and `plan = plan_on_day[days[0]]` (line **2678**) raises `IndexError: list index out of range`. `days[0]` is also used at line 2679 (`plan_start`) and line 2697 (`first_plan_day = days[0]`), and `days[-1]` at 2698.

**No empty-results guard protects this.** The only early `continue` before this point is the `if sc.options.only_warn:` branch at lines 2649-2652; there is no `if not results:` / `if not plan_on_day:` check. Downstream, `plan_over_time` (built from these) and `plan_on_day[ymd]` (line 2707) feed the plan-recommendation and traffic-graph sections, all of which assume at least one traffic day exists.</result>

# U-M institution-specific logic in `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

Main script: `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (3756 lines). Context module: `/workspace/script_context.py` (92 lines). All line numbers below are current.

## 1. The existing `[UMich].enabled` guard pattern

The canonical three-part guard `"UMich" in sc.config and "enabled" in sc.config["UMich"] and sc.config["UMich"]["enabled"]` appears in **three** places in the core script, plus in the two `umich` package `__init__.py` files.

**Guard A — recipient resolution / portal-membership check** (`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails:1053-1063`):
```python
1053        portal_site_id = 0
1054        if (
1055            "UMich" in sc.config
1056            and "enabled" in sc.config["UMich"]
1057            and sc.config["UMich"]["enabled"]
1058        ):
1059            if site["name"] not in sc.config["UMich"]["portal"]["sites"]:
1060                sc.console.print(
1061                    f":exclamation: [bold red] ATTENTION: {site['name']} is not in the WWS portal!"
1062                )
1063                continue
1064            portal_site_id = sc.config["UMich"]["portal"]["sites"][site["name"]]["id"]
```

**Guard B — recipient/owner-group + the annual-billing subject line** (`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails:3436-3472`):
```python

...

```
and the second, date-driven billing guard immediately after:

## 3. Config structure &amp; extensibility

**`sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`** (`/workspace/sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`, 126 lines) has **NO `[UMich]`, `[Email]`, or `[SMTP]` section at all.** Its only sections are `[Pantheon]`, `[Pantheon.plan_info.*]`, `[Pantheon.plan_sku_to_name]`, `[Database]`, `[Cloudflare]` (L99, `enabled = false`), `[AWS]` (L107, `enabled = false`), and `[News]` (L115). So in the sample config `"UMich" in sc.config` is False and every guard evaluates false.

**The live `[UMich]` section** exists only in `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` (a symlink into `pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config/`), L105-113:
```toml
105  [UMich]
106  enabled=true
107  [UMich.portal]
108  [UMich.portal.db]
109  host = "&lt;{secret aws webinfo db_host}"
110  port = 3306
111  user = "&lt;{secret aws webinfo db_user}"
112  password = "&lt;{secret aws webinfo db_pass}"
113  name = "&lt;{secret aws webinfo db_name}"
```
Note `[UMich].portal.sites`, `owner_group`, `shortcode`, and `id` are **not** in the TOML — they are populated at runtime by `setup_portal_db()` from the MySQL portal DB (see `plugin/umich/portal.py:59`, `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['sites'] = portal_sites`).

**Answer to your key question:** There is currently **no `[Email].from`, `[Email].reply_to`, `[SMTP].host`, or any email/SMTP config anywhere.** All of From/Reply-to/Bcc/SMTP-host/message-id-domain are hardcoded Python string literals (Section 2 i, a, h). Moving them out would mean introducing **new config keys** (e.g. a new `[Email]` and/or `[SMTP]` section), not repurposing existing ones.

**The substitution / hook machinery** (the seams you'd use to move logic into the `umich` packages):

`/workspace/script_context.py` defines the registries and helpers:
```python
18  substitutions = []
20  hooks = { 'setup': [], 'check': [], }
25  plugin_context = {}
39  def add_hook(hook_name: str, target: dict) -&gt; None:
40      if hook_name in hooks:
41          hooks[hook_name].append(target)
42      else:
43          hooks[hook_name] = [target]
46  def invoke_hooks(hook_name: str, *args, **kwargs) -&gt; None:
...
49          for hook in hooks[hook_name]:
51              hook['func'](*args, **kwargs)
```
(`script_context.py` also has `add_notice`, `add_news_item` helpers around L60-85.)

`config_substitution()` / `process_config()` (`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails:667-750`): `process_config` recursively walks the loaded config and replaces `&lt;{...}&gt;` tokens (regex `config_substitution_re = re.compile(r"&lt;\{(.*?)(?&lt;!\\)}")`, L732). `config_substitution` scans `sc.substitutions` for the best-matching registered pattern (each entry is `{'args': [...], 'func': ..., 'func_args': [...]}`, matching literal tokens and `$var` captures) and calls its `func`. This is how `"&lt;{umich portal plan_info 'Basic' cost}"` in the live TOML resolves via the `plan_info` function registered in `plugin/umich/__init__.py:8-12`. Note `process_config` runs **twice** — pre-setup (L903) and post-setup (L934) — so substitutions that depend on DB data (`setup_completed` gate in `portal.py:70-73`) resolve on the second pass.

**Plugin/check loading** (`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails:896-909` in `main()`): `find_modules("plugin")` / `find_modules("check")` walk the dirs for `__init__.py` files and `importlib.import_module` them. Import-time code in each `__init__.py` self-registers via `sc.add_hook` / `sc.substitutions.append`. Hooks are fired by `sc.invoke_hooks("setup")` (L931) and there is a `check` hook list; `check.umich.sitelens` registers two `check` hooks and one `setup.umich.portal` hook.

**Current contents of `plugin/umich/`:**
- `/workspace/plugin/umich/__init__.py` (12 lines) — guard + registers `setup` hook `plugin.umich.portal.setup_portal_db` and the `umich portal plan_info` substitution.
- `/workspace/plugin/umich/portal.py` (73 lines) — `setup_portal_db()` reads `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['db']`, queries `sites_site` / `sites_pantheonplan` tables, populates `portal_sites` (id/owner_group/shortcode), `portal_plan_info`, and `sc.config['Pantheon']['plan_sku_to_name']`; fires `setup.umich.portal` hook; `plan_info(plan, field)` substitution function.

**Current contents of `check/umich/`:**
- `/workspace/check/umich/__init__.py` (11 lines) — guard + registers `setup.umich.portal`, `check` (urls), `check` (scores) hooks; else prints skip message.
- `/workspace/check/umich/sitelens.py` (246 lines) — `setup_sitelens(connection)`, `check_sitelens_urls(site_context)`, `check_sitelens_scores(site_context)`, `create_gauge_image()`. Reads `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['sites']`, builds Lighthouse gauge images, and appends attachments/sections to `site_context`. Hardcodes `admin.webservices.umich.edu` URLs (L116, L219) and `make_msgid(domain='webservices.umich.edu')` (L207).

The pattern is clear: the `umich` **check** package already uses `site_context` mutation via hooks (`add_notice`, `site_context['sections']`, `site_context['attachments']`) — that is the intended seam for moving the inline U-M checks (Sections 2 b/c/d/e/f) out of the core loop.

## 4. Riskiest items to move (byte-for-byte golden-output risk)

Ranked by how likely a refactor is to change rendered `build/{site}.html`, `build/{site}.txt`, or `build/{site}.eml` output:

**Highest risk — output changes byte-for-byte if touched:**

1. **MIME headers block (L3661-3671)** and **`make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` (L3587-3588, and sitelens L207).** These write directly into the `.eml`. `make_msgid` already produces a random left-hand side each run, but the **domain suffix** is in the golden. If you move `From`/`Reply-to`/`Bcc`/message-id-domain to config, the default values must reproduce the exact strings (`University of Michigan Webmaster Team &lt;webmaster@umich.edu&gt;`, `webmaster@umich.edu`, `januside@go.mail.umich.edu, its-webmaster@go.mail.umich.edu`, and dry-run `To:` string) character-for-character, including the `Reply-to` capitalization (not the RFC-usual `Reply-To`).

2. **The two annual-billing notices (Guard B L3466-3540 and Guard C L3552-3585).** These insert a notice at position 0 of `sorted_notices`, which also drives the **subject line** (`Time Sensitive: … annual billing` / `Action Required: …`). The HTML/text bodies contain exact dollar-formatting (`${annual_bill:,.2f}`), dates, shortcodes, and `admin.webservices.umich.edu/sites/{portal_site_id}/...` URLs. Any reordering, whitespace, or wording change shifts the golden. These are also date-driven, so the golden depends on the run date.

3. **`umich-oidc-login` reinstall notice (L1707-1792)** and **UMich Hummingbird notice (L1823-1861).** Large multi-line HTML+text f-strings appended to `site_notices`; whitespace and the embedded `terminus wp {site}.dev` command are load-bearing for byte-identical output. The `semver.compare(p["version"], "1.2.99") &lt;= 0` threshold determines *whether* the notice fires — changing the gating condition changes which sites get the notice.

**Medium risk — output changes only for sites that have Cloudflare FQDNs:**

4. **`umich-cloudflare` WP check (L1681-1689)** and **Drupal cloudflare-module checks (L2010-2043)** — gated by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) &gt; 0`. If you move the gating logic or the `node/5114` / `node/4242` doc URLs into config, the produced notices (short/message/text) must match exactly. The doc-URL strings are embedded via `check_wordpress_plugin` / `check_drupal_module` args, so they surface into notice bodies.

5. **Drupal user-agent check (L2201-2265)** — the `startswith("Drupal (+https://drupal.org/); UMich; https://")` test and the `node/4242` notice. Refactoring the expected UA prefix or the `ifconfig.me/ua` probe changes which sites get flagged and thus the golden.

**Lower risk — dormant or non-rendered:**

6. **`smtp_login()` (L769-773)** — only referenced from commented-out send code (L3710-3713); moving/parameterizing it will not change any golden output today. Safe to refactor first.

7. **`lsa-disko-project` / `umma-inside-wp` special-case (L3444-3446)** — already inside Guard B, only affects the `recipients`/`To:` header for two specific U-M sites; low blast radius but *does* change the `.eml` `To:` for those two sites if altered, so preserve exactly when U-M-enabled.

**Note on the `[UMich]`-guarded blocks vs the un-guarded ones:** the golden production run has `[UMich].enabled = true`, so *all* of the above execute in the golden. But the un-guarded items (2a-f) are exactly the ones that would also fire — or crash — on a hypothetical non-U-M run today (e.g. the `fqdns_behind_cloudflare`-gated Cloudflare checks emit U-M doc URLs to any institution). Those are the cleanest candidates to relocate into the `umich` plugin/check packages behind the existing hook seams, because doing so removes U-M output from non-U-M runs **without** changing the U-M golden (the same functions, invoked via hooks, produce the same notices).</result>

# GOAL 1 — P9 (WCAG `link-name`)

## Anchors in `email_template.html`

Every `&lt;a&gt;` in `/workspace/email_template.html` (grep of `&lt;a href=...&gt;` and the `&lt;a&gt;...&lt;img&gt;` pattern):

| Line | Anchor | Discernible text? |
|---|---|---|
| **262** | `&lt;a href="https://its.umich.edu/" target="_blank"&gt;&lt;img alt="U-M Information and Technology Services" class="banner_image" src="cid:{{banner_cid}}" .../&gt;&lt;/a&gt;` | Wraps **only an `&lt;img&gt;`** — but the img has a non-empty `alt`, so it is technically named. This is the only image-wrapping anchor in the static template. |
| 289 | `...U-M Pantheon website&lt;/a&gt;` and `&lt;a href="{{site_url}}"&gt;{{site_url}}&lt;/a&gt;` | Yes (text) |
| 290 | `ITS Web Hosting Services Portal`, `obtain support through either Pantheon or ITS` | Yes |
| 334 | `U-M Pantheon pricing` | Yes |
| 336 | `Upgrade to a higher plan` | Yes |
| 340 | `Downgrade to Basic`, `Performance plan features` | Yes |
| 342 | `Downgrade to a lower plan` | Yes |
| 344 | `Pantheon visitors, which are much lower...` | Yes |
| 356 | `&lt;a href="{{site_url}}"&gt;{{site_url}}&lt;/a&gt;` (in `&lt;caption&gt;`) | Yes |
| 422 | `Estimated Pantheon Website Cost graph` | Yes |
| 435 | `&lt;a href="mailto:webmaster@umich.edu"&gt;webmaster@umich.edu&lt;/a&gt;` | Yes |

Note: line **351** is a bare `&lt;img class="chart_image" alt="Chart showing Pantheon website traffic over time..."&gt;` — it has a good `alt` and is **not** inside an anchor.

Key point: In the *static* template, no anchor is unambiguously text-less — line 262 wraps an img but that img carries `alt`. So the `link-name` violation axe reports on **both** the WordPress and Drupal reports (per PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md P9) most plausibly comes from a **runtime-injected** section, not the static file. See below.

## `email_template.txt`
Plain-text template — no `&lt;a&gt;`/`&lt;img&gt;` markup; not an accessibility surface. (No anchors found.)

## Runtime-injected images/anchors in `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

- CIDs are created with `make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` at **L3587–3588** (`banner_cid`, `chart_cid`), passed to the template as `banner_cid=banner_cid[1:-1]` / `chart_cid=chart_cid[1:-1]`. The `alt` text for these lives **in the template** (lines 262, 351), not in the program.
- The program builds inline-image HTML for **SiteLens gauges** in `/workspace/check/umich/sitelens.py` via `create_gauge_image(value, color, label) -&gt; PNG bytes`. Per `tests/integration/test_check_sitelens.py` (L50–79), `check_sitelens_scores(ctx)` appends one inline PNG attachment per score (`maintype=image`, `subtype=png`, `disposition=inline`, each with a `cid`) and emits a `SiteLens` section whose `content` references the images by `cid:` (asserted `.count("cid:") == 4`). **The tests assert the `cid` wiring but never assert `alt` text** — this is the most likely source of the runtime `link-name` violation if any gauge image is wrapped in an anchor without an accessible name.
- Other program-generated anchors are all text links (e.g. L571/587/659 plugin-install messages, L3263/3298/3480/3501 portal links) — none wrap bare images.
- Matplotlib chart: rendered with `fig.savefig(buf, format="png")` at **L3058**; attached by CID, alt supplied by the template.

## Render test — `/workspace/tests/render/test_render.py`

- `_AXE_ALLOWLIST = {"color-contrast", "region", "link-name"}` at **L34**. Confirmed it includes `link-name`. The comment (L30–33) explicitly labels `link-name` a **pre-existing template defect (P9)**, allowlisted only so the smoke still catches NEW regressions.
- axe is vendored: `_AXE = .../tests/vendor/axe.min.js` (L24), injected via `page.add_script_tag(path=str(_AXE))` (L85), run with `axe.run(document)` (L86).
- Gating (L87–93): collects violations where `v["impact"] in ("serious","critical")` **and** `v["id"] not in _AXE_ALLOWLIST`, then `assert not serious`. So serious/critical fail the test **unless** allowlisted. The test is parametrized over both `rendered_report` and `rendered_report_drupal` (L55).
- CID handling: `_rewrite_cids_to_local` (L37–52) extracts inline images from the `.eml` and rewrites `cid:` refs to local `file://` URIs so a standalone Chromium can resolve them.
- If Chromium can't launch → `pytest.skip` with the exact setup hint (L66–67), not a failure.

# GOAL 2 — Test harness map

## Fixtures (all in `/workspace/tests/conftest.py`)

| Fixture | Def line | Scope | Provides |
|---|---|---|---|
| `psh` | L85–88 | session | The loaded program module (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails` via `SourceFileLoader`, cached once). |
| `reset_sc(psh)` | L104–125 | **autouse** | Deep-copies/restores `script_context` mutable globals (`options, config, news, hooks, substitutions, plugin, check, plugin_context`) around each test; `yield`s the `sc` module (L125). |
| `temp_db(psh, tmp_path)` | L145–149 | function | `TempDB` = fresh sqlite engine + `Session` + ORM models (`PantheonTraffic`, `PantheonOverageProtection`); disposes engine on teardown. No repo DB touched. |
| `rendered_report(tmp_path_factory)` | L259–264 | session | Runs the full offline shim pipeline for WordPress `its-wws-test1`; returns artifacts dict (`work`, `proc`, plus `html`/`txt`/`eml` paths from `_rendered_artifacts`, L246). |
| `rendered_report_drupal(tmp_path_factory)` | L267–274 | session | Same for Drupal `its-wws-test2` (passes `fixtures_dir=TERMINUS_FIXTURES_DRUPAL`). |
| `program_runner()` | L424–427 | function | Returns the `run_program` callable. |
| `forbidden_flag_error()` | L430–434 | function | Returns the `ForbiddenFlagError` class (for `pytest.raises`). |
| `forbidden_live_data_error()` | L437–441 | function | Returns the `ForbiddenLiveDataError` class. |
| `normalize_html()` | L444–447 | function | Returns `normalize_report_html` (CID-normalizer for goldens). |

Module-level helpers (not fixtures) also in conftest: `seed_traffic(db_path, *, site_id, year=2026, month=3, plan="Performance Small")` (L196), `build_rendered_report(work, *, site, site_id, fixtures_dir=None)` (L216), `normalize_report_html(text)` (L191, replaces volatile `make_msgid` CIDs with `cid:NORMALIZED`). There is no fixture literally named `minimal_config` or `run_program`/`seed_traffic` — `MINIMAL_CONFIG` is a module constant (L179 = `CONFIG_DIR/"minimal.toml"`), `run_program` is a plain function exposed via the `program_runner` fixture, and `seed_traffic` is a plain function.

## Safety interlock in `run_program()` (conftest L390–414)

`run_program(args, *, cwd, mode="replay", extra_env=None, timeout=300, fixtures_dir=None)` calls two guards before exec:

- **`ForbiddenFlagError`** — `_assert_flags_allowed(args)` (L296): raises if a token is in `FORBIDDEN_FLAGS = {"--all","-a","--for-real"}` (L52), OR is an argparse abbreviation prefix of a forbidden long flag (`--al`, `--fo`, `--for`), OR appears in a short-flag bundle (`-av`, `-va`). Message from `_forbidden_msg` (L289). This is constraints **C1/C2**.
- **`ForbiddenLiveDataError`** — `_assert_offline_data_flags(args, mode, cwd)` (L349): triggered by `OFFLINE_ONLY_DATA_FLAGS = ("--create-tables","--import-older-metrics")` when **either** (a) `mode == "live"` (L92–95: "may create/modify the production database"), **or** (b) the effective `--config` does not resolve under the fixture allowlist `_CONFIG_ALLOWLIST_ROOTS = (CONFIG_DIR,)` plus the run's own `cwd` (L376–382). Deliberately a **config-PATH allowlist check, not a backend-type test** — the production default DB is also sqlite, so an "is-it-sqlite?" test would fail open (constraint C2). `_resolve_config_arg` (L319) mirrors argparse exactly, including stopping at `--`.

After the guards, it prepends `SHIM_DIR` to `PATH`, sets `TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR` (= `fixtures_dir` or default `TERMINUS_FIXTURES`), `TERMINUS_SHIM_MODE`, `TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL`, `MPLBACKEND=Agg`, and returns a `subprocess.CompletedProcess`.

Interlock tests: `/workspace/tests/unit/test_interlock.py` — forbidden flags incl. abbreviations/bundles (L19/21/26), allowed flags don't raise (L31), Part C live-mode refusal (L47), non-fixture-config refusal (L55), offline+fixture allowed (L64), and the post-`--` bypass attempt is refused (L80–88).

## The two goldens

- **WordPress** `its-wws-test1` (`E2E_SITE`, id `9cf2c790-...`, conftest L175–176) → fixtures in `tests/fixtures/terminus/`; golden `tests/e2e/__snapshots__/test_golden.ambr`. Tests: `tests/e2e/test_golden.py` (`test_rendered_html_matches_golden` L12, `test_rendered_txt_matches_golden` L17).
- **Drupal** `its-wws-test2` (`E2E_SITE2`, id `acb22aef-...`, conftest L183–185) → fixtures in `tests/fixtures/terminus-drupal/`; golden `tests/e2e/__snapshots__/test_golden_drupal.ambr`. Tests: `tests/e2e/test_golden_drupal.py` (L13/21/26).
- Selection: `build_rendered_report(..., fixtures_dir=...)` passes `fixtures_dir` through to `run_program`, which sets `TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR`. The Drupal fixture uses `fixtures_dir=TERMINUS_FIXTURES_DRUPAL`; default (WordPress) uses `TERMINUS_FIXTURES`.
- `--update-goldens` → `run-tests` L41–42 adds `--snapshot-update` (syrupy). `--record` → `run-tests` L28–29 shells out to `tests/tools/record.py`. `record.py --drupal` (L106) records `its-wws-test2` into `fixtures/terminus-drupal` (WordPress default → `fixtures/terminus`); it runs the program LIVE (read-only) with the shim in `record` mode, then `scrub()`s (L44) org/domain/team fixtures for commit-safety.

## Marks / tiers

Marks: `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow` (tests/README.md L54). `./run-tests --fast` adds `-m "not live and not slow"` (`run-tests` L33–34); full run includes everything (incl. `live`, which needs Terminus auth + network). Other `run-tests` flags: `--llm` (L35–38, terse machine summary via the `pytest_terminal_summary` hook at conftest L460), `--coverage` (L39, no gate, in-process tiers only), passthrough of any other args to pytest (L44). Directory→tier map: `unit/`, `integration/`, `e2e/`, `live/`, `render/`, `email/` (README L44–49).

## ⚠️ Correction on the "strict-`xfail`" tests for P2 / P3 / P6

**There are NO `pytest.mark.xfail` markers anywhere in the test suite.** A repo-wide grep for `xfail`/`xpass` over `tests/**/*.py` matched only `tests/conftest.py:471` — the `xfailed=/xpassed=` counters in the `--llm` summary hook. So nothing will "flip to xpass" automatically. What actually exists:

- **P6 (wrapper 3-tuple)** — real, passing characterization tests in `/workspace/tests/integration/test_wrappers.py`. Docstring L4–5 states they pin the **actual** 3-tuple `(result, errors, fatal)` while the program docstrings still declare 2-tuples. Tests: `test_wp_parses_json_three_tuple` (L22), `test_wp_bad_json_returns_none_and_keeps_errors` (L30), `test_wp_eval_strips_and_three_tuple` (L37), `test_drush_parses_json_three_tuple` (L45), `test_drush_moves_leading_noise_to_errors` (L52), `test_drush_php_script_passes_script_as_input` (L60). These will keep **passing** when P6 is fixed (only the program's docstrings change), so they are not xfail and won't flip.

- **P3 (`terminus()` should return `(result, errors, fatal)`)** — PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md P3 (L73, "Test coverage now") *claims* "a strict-`xfail` documents the desired `(result, errors, fatal)` contract." **That strict-xfail was never implemented.** What exists instead is `/workspace/tests/integration/test_regressions.py` `test_terminus_retries_on_expired_session` (L21) and `test_terminus_retry_does_not_loop_forever` (L38), which pin the **current** single-value contract — `assert result == {"ok": 1}` (L34), i.e. `terminus()` returns only the parsed result, not a tuple. When P3 is fixed to return a 3-tuple, **these tests will break** (`result` becomes a tuple) and must be rewritten — they are the opposite of an xfail-that-passes. This is the gap you'll want to fill when planning additions.

- **P2 (config-inline `[News]` never added, dead `continue` loop at program L863–870)** — **no test exists at all.** No test in the suite references `news`/`add_news_item` as a behavior under test (the only hits are `reset_sc` restoring `sc.news` and the workdir creating an empty `news/` dir). P2 has **zero** coverage; there is nothing to flip.

Only three test files name P-numbers: `test_wrappers.py:5` (P6), `test_render.py:31` (P9), `test_recommendation_e2e.py:5` (P1). P2 and P3 are named in no test.

## Bottom line for planning test additions
- The `link-name` (P9) fix needs an `alt`/`aria-label` on whatever bare-image anchor axe flags. The static template's only image-anchor (L262) already has `alt`; the flagged violation is almost certainly the **runtime SiteLens gauge** path in `check/umich/sitelens.py`, whose tests (`test_check_sitelens.py`) currently assert `cid` wiring but not accessible names. When you fix P9, remove `link-name` from `_AXE_ALLOWLIST` (test_render.py L34).
- Your premise about "strict-xfail tests that flip to xpass" does not match the code: **no xfail tests exist.** P6 has passing characterization tests (won't flip), P3's claimed strict-xfail was never written (the existing regression tests will *break* on fix), and P2 has no test at all. Plan accordingly — you may want to *add* the strict-xfail for P3 and any test for P2 as part of the work.</result>

# Adversarial Review: Fix P1–P10 plan

I verified against `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails`, `script_context.py`, the tests, templates, and `minimal.toml`. Several load-bearing claims hold; two are contradicted by the code, and the P8/non-U-M verification story is broken.

## Verified as accurate
- **P3 call-site count is correct.** Exactly 10 `terminus()` call sites (487, 925, 1030, 1084, 1153, 1193, 1318, 2130, 2276, 3449). The only other match is the internal recursive retry `return terminus(*args)` at L351, which propagates the new 3-tuple naturally. Feasibility (c): the enumeration is complete.
- **`terminus()` current contract** matches the plan: single-value return, `result = ""` on `JSONDecodeError`, commented `# return result, errors.strip(), fatal # TODO` at L352. `wp()`/`drush()` already return real 3-tuples (P6 is docstring-only). Confirmed.
- **`add_notice` byte-identical migration is feasible (feasibility a).** All 25 *live* notice dicts and all 4 builder helpers already carry `type`/`icon`/`text`/`message`; none carry `order`. So `add_notice`'s icon/text/order defaults are genuine no-ops → append is byte-identical. The plan's caution is well-founded and achievable.
- **No strict-xfail tests exist for P2/P3** (grep confirms). The plan correctly overrides the problems-doc's false claim. `test_regressions.py`'s two retry tests do unpack `result = terminus(...)` single-value and will break under P3 — correctly flagged.
- **`Reply-to` capitalization (feasibility b, mechanically):** `msg["Reply-to"] = ...` — `EmailMessage` preserves header-name case, so reading the value from config reproduces the exact byte. Mechanically sound.

---

## 1. Completeness — ISSUES

**1a. [Completeness] P3 test rewrite omits `test_terminus_seam.py`.** The plan only names `test_regressions.py` for rewrite, but `tests/integration/test_terminus_seam.py` also pins the single-value contract (L16 `== {"framework": "wordpress"}`) **and the `""`-on-decode behavior** (L22 `assert psh.terminus("env:info", "x") == ""`). Both assertions break the moment P3 returns a 3-tuple / `None`. `tests/live/test_live_smoke.py` (L14, L19) likewise unpacks single-value. *Fix:* add `test_terminus_seam.py` (and the live smoke) to the P3 rewrite list in the plan and in step 4.

**1b. [Completeness] `add_notice` migration miscounts.** L2546's `site_notices.append` is inside a fully commented-out block (dead). Live appends = **25, not 26**. Harmless but means the plan's checklist number is off; state it as "25 live appends (L2546 is dead/commented)".

## 2. Consistency — BLOCKING ISSUE

**2a. [Consistency — BLOCKING] The non-U-M golden assertion contradicts P8's pragmatic-subset scope.** The plan (test spec, L271–273) says the non-U-M render "contains **no** `umich.edu` / `node/5114` / `webmaster@umich.edu` strings." But `email_template.html` **hardcodes** U-M content that P8's pragmatic subset explicitly does not touch (no `&lt;{ }&gt;` substitution in the template):
- L262 `https://its.umich.edu/` (banner), L289/290/334/336/340/342 `its.umich.edu/...` and `admin.webservices.umich.edu/...`, L422 `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4705`, and **L289 + L435 literal `webmaster@umich.edu`**.

`minimal.toml` already has **no `[UMich]` section** (UMich effectively disabled), yet the current golden `.ambr` contains **22 umich strings and 7 distinct U-M URLs** — all from the static template, all outside P8's scope. So a non-U-M golden asserting "no `umich.edu`" and "no `webmaster@umich.edu`" will **fail** against P8-pragmatic output. The decision ("non-U-M run emits no U-M content") and the P8 pragmatic subset are mutually inconsistent. *Fix:* either (a) narrow the non-U-M golden to assert only the strings P8 actually removes (the `node/5114`/`node/4242` CF doc-URLs and the moved MIME headers), and add an explicit "template still carries U-M branding — deferred" note to NOT-in-scope; or (b) pull the template's hardcoded U-M URLs into `[Email]`/config too (a real scope increase — reject unless intended). As written the plan overstates what the non-U-M golden proves.

**2b. [Consistency] P4 design changes notice aggregation without saying so.** The existing "not in DNS" notice is a **single aggregated** notice over all `not_in_dns` hosts (L1592–1611). The plan's `classify_hostname_dns` diagram emits a **per-host** `notice(type=alert, "&lt;host&gt; is not in DNS")`. That is a rendering change (one combined notice → N per-host notices). Golden-neutral offline (no `not_in_dns` hosts), but the plan should state whether it keeps the L1592 aggregated notice or replaces it. *Fix:* make P4 append transient/definitive *diagnostic* notices but keep the existing aggregated `not_in_dns` notice unchanged, or explicitly declare the aggregation change.

## 3. Clarity — ISSUES

**3a. [Clarity] "4 builders → `add_notice`" is mechanically ambiguous.** The builders (`wp_error`, `drush_error`, `check_wordpress_plugin`, `check_drupal_module`) **return `list[dict]`**; callers do `site_notices += builder(...)` (L1665, 1969, etc.). They never append. "Route through `add_notice`" is undefined for a function that builds-and-returns. *Fix:* specify the mechanism — either keep builders returning lists and route the *caller's* `+=` through `add_notice` in a loop, or pass the target list into the builder. (Either is byte-identical since dicts are complete.)

**3b. [Clarity] Step 3 "extract `build_plan_over_time`" under-states coupling.** `plan_on_day` feeds *multiple* downstream consumers, not just span-building: L2677–2707 (spans, `first_plan_day = days[0]`) **and** L3106 `plan = plan_on_day[d]` in a later loop. The empty-guard itself is trivial, but "extract a pure `build_plan_over_time(plan_on_day, plot_right_date) -&gt; list`" cleanly separable (feasibility d) is optimistic — the function's output isn't the only thing derived from `plan_on_day`. *Fix:* scope the extraction to just the span computation and keep the empty-guard (`if not plan_on_day: notice+skip`) inline; don't claim full separability.

## 4. Scope — ISSUES

**4a. [Scope — under-scoped] P8a omits the `@umich.edu` suffix on the dry-run recipient.** The dry-run `To` is `f"januside@go.mail.umich.edu, {sc.options.smtp_username}@umich.edu"` (L3667–3668). The plan's `[Email].dry_run_to` captures only the fixed `januside@…` prefix; the hardcoded `@umich.edu` domain appended to `smtp_username` is **not** configurable. For U-M it's byte-identical (fine), but it defeats P8's reusability goal and contributes another `umich.edu` string to any non-U-M render/`.eml`. This is also why the existing `test_eml_is_addressed…` passes on `testuser@umich.edu`. *Fix:* add a config key for the dry-run username domain (e.g. `[Email].dry_run_username_domain`), or document it as a known remaining U-M hardcode in NOT-in-scope.

## 5. Feasibility — BLOCKING + ISSUES

**5a. [Feasibility — BLOCKING] P8b relocation into "the existing check-hook seam" is sequenced wrong.** `sc.invoke_hooks("check", site_context)` fires at **L1293** — *before* `fqdns_behind_cloudflare` is even initialized (L1325) and populated (L1421), and *before* the WP `installed_plugins` / Drupal module data that the CF checks consume (`check_wordpress_plugin("umich-cloudflare", …)` at L1682; Drupal at L2011–2040). The plan says "Same functions, invoked via the existing check-hook seam → U-M golden unchanged." That is **not possible** at the L1293 seam — the hook would run before the data it needs exists. *Fix:* P8b requires a **new** hook invocation point placed after DNS resolution and framework-data gathering (e.g. a `post_gather` hook per site), or the CF-check inputs must be threaded into `site_context` before L1293. Either way it is more than a "move"; the plan must add the hook seam. (This is the single most under-analyzed item.)

**5b. [Feasibility — BLOCKING] There is no `.eml` golden to verify P8a against.** The plan repeatedly instructs "verify the `.eml` golden byte-identical" (P8a design, step 8, Verification section). **No such golden exists.** The goldens are HTML (CID-normalized) + TXT only (`test_golden.py`). The `.eml` is checked only by existence + one substring (`"testuser@umich.edu" in eml`, `test_shim_e2e.py`). Moreover `msg["Date"] = datetime.now(UTC)` (L3672) is volatile, which is presumably *why* no byte `.eml` golden exists. Consequently: (i) the MIME headers P8a moves (`From`/`Reply-to`/`Bcc`/`To`) are currently **unguarded** by any golden — a regression won't be caught; (ii) the plan's stated verification mechanism is fictional. *Fix:* before P8a, **add** a targeted `.eml` header test (or a normalized `.eml` golden that scrubs `Date:` and the `make_msgid` CIDs) asserting the exact `From`/`Reply-to`/`Bcc`/dry-run-`To`/`Message-ID` bytes; only then is "byte-identical" a checkable claim.

**5c. [Feasibility — minor] P9 diagnosis is likely wrong (mitigated).** The plan's primary hypothesis — the SiteLens gauge anchor "never has an accessible name" — is contradicted by `check/umich/sitelens.py` L219–220: the gauge anchor wraps an `&lt;img … alt="{label}: {value} / 100"&gt;` (non-empty alt), and the static banner anchor (L262) also has non-empty alt. So neither obvious candidate is the `link-name` culprit; the real offender is elsewhere. The plan does mandate "reproduce first" (`-m render`, inspect the axe node), which saves it — but the stated hypothesis should be dropped so the implementer doesn't "fix" an already-accessible anchor and re-enable the allowlist prematurely. *Fix:* replace the speculative hypothesis with "identify the flagged node via axe before editing."

**5d. [Feasibility — positive note] `load_news_items` is clean and also fixes a latent bug.** Confirmed L977–993. Note the *current* folder loop at L986 does `glob.glob(f"{sc.config['News']['folder']}/*.toml")` **outside** the `if "News" in sc.config` guard → `KeyError` if `[News]` is absent. The plan's `sc.config.get("News", {}).get("folder")` silently fixes that. Fine, but call it out as an intended behavior change (no-`[News]` goes from crash to no-op) so it isn't mistaken for a golden-affecting regression.

---

## Quality score: **6 / 10**

Well-structured, honestly self-corrects the problems doc, and most mechanical claims (10 call sites, add_notice byte-identity, terminus contract) verify. But it has two genuinely blocking defects (P8b hook sequencing; the phantom `.eml` golden that P8a's verification depends on), a hard consistency break between the non-U-M golden goal and the pragmatic-subset scope, and several missed test files / under-scoped hardcodes.

## Verdict: **NOT PASS** — blocking issues:

1. **[Consistency, BLOCKING]** Non-U-M golden's "no `umich.edu`/`webmaster@umich.edu`" assertion is unachievable under P8-pragmatic because `email_template.html` hardcodes ~7 U-M URLs + `webmaster@umich.edu` (L262/289/290/334/422/435), none in scope. Narrow the assertion to P8-removed strings and document the template as remaining U-M debt.
2. **[Feasibility, BLOCKING]** P8b cannot use the existing check hook (fires L1293, before `fqdns_behind_cloudflare` @1325/1421 and plugin data @1665+). Add a new post-gather hook seam.
3. **[Feasibility, BLOCKING]** No `.eml` golden exists (HTML+TXT only; `Date:` is volatile). Add a normalized `.eml`/header assertion test before P8a; the current "verify .eml golden" steps reference nothing.
4. **[Completeness]** P3 rewrite must also cover `test_terminus_seam.py` (pins single-value + `== ""`) and `test_live_smoke.py`, not just `test_regressions.py`.
5. **[Scope, under-scoped]** P8a leaves `{smtp_username}@umich.edu` hardcoded (L3668); either make the domain configurable or document it.
6. **[Clarity]** Define the mechanism for routing the 4 return-a-list builders through `add_notice`; correct the "26 appends" count to 25 live (L2546 is commented out).
7. **[Consistency/Clarity]** State whether P4 keeps the aggregated `not_in_dns` notice (L1592) or replaces it with per-host notices.
8. **[Feasibility, minor]** Drop the falsified P9 SiteLens-gauge hypothesis (its `&lt;img&gt;` already has `alt`); rely on the reproduce-first step.</result>

```
246	(`check/umich/sitelens.py` L219–220) wraps an `<img … alt="{label}: {value} / 100">`. The real
247	offending node is elsewhere. **Implementation MUST first reproduce** (`./run-tests -m render`,
248	inspect the exact axe `link-name` node/target) to identify the flagged anchor, then give it
249	discernible text — a non-empty `img alt` or `aria-label`. Then remove `link-name` from
250	`_AXE_ALLOWLIST` (`tests/render/test_render.py` L34) so the a11y smoke enforces it. Verify with
251	`./run-tests -m render` green.
252	
253	### P10 — `IndexError` on zero traffic (current L2654–2698)
254	`plan_on_day` is populated only inside `for row in results:`. Zero in-window rows → `plan_on_day={}`
255	→ `days = sorted(plan_on_day.keys())` `[]` → `plan_on_day[days[0]]` raises `IndexError`.
256	
257	**Extraction for testability:** `build_plan_over_time(plan_on_day, plot_right_date) -> list`
258	(pure; returns `[]` for empty input). `main()`: if `not plan_on_day`, `sc.add_notice(type=info,
259	"No traffic recorded yet for this site.")`, skip the plan/recommendation + traffic-graph sections
260	gracefully (same "new site" clean state as P1), and do not index `days[0]`.
261	Shadow paths: empty (zero traffic) → notice + skip; single day → one span; normal → unchanged.
262	
263	### `add_notice` canonical migration (golden-sensitive)
264	- Adapt `sc.add_notice(notice, notices_list)` (or keep `site_context` but ensure it targets the same
265	  `site_notices` list) so it is usable **before** `site_context` is built (many appends precede
266	  L1289) and **inside** the builder helpers (which have no `site_context`).
267	- Route the 26 direct `site_notices.append({...})` sites and the 4 builders (`wp_error`,
268	  `drush_error`, `check_wordpress_plugin`, `check_drupal_module`) through `add_notice`.
269	- **Preserve every notice dict's existing keys** so `add_notice`'s `icon`/`text`/`order` defaults are
270	  no-ops where those keys are already present → byte-identical. Any golden diff means a dict relied
271	  on a default differently; investigate before proceeding. Do this as an isolated commit verified by
272	  both U-M goldens; if a given site cannot migrate byte-identically, leave it raw and note it.
273
```

Fix by iterating `.items()` and skipping non-dict **values**\n(the scalar `folder` directive), then adding each `[News.<x>]` subtable.\n\n**Extraction for testability:** move both loaders (config-inline + `*.toml` files) into a\nmodule-level `load_news_items()` that reads `sc.config` / `sc.options` and populates `sc.news`\n(behavior-preserving for the file path). `main()` calls `psh.load_news_items()`.\n\n```python\ndef load_news_items() -> None:\n    if \"News\" in sc.config:\n        for name, value in sc.config[\"News\"].items():\n            if not isinstance(value, dict):   # skip 'folder' and other scalar directives\n                continue\n            sc.add_news_item(value, f\"{name} in configuration file {sc.options.config}\")\n    folder = sc.config.get(\"News\", {}).get(\"folder\")\n    if folder:\n        for filename in sorted(glob.glob(f\"{folder}/*.toml\")):\n            ...  # unchanged file loader\n```\nShadow paths: no `[News]` table → no-op; only `folder` key → nothing added; `[News.<x>]` missing\n`message` → existing `add_news_item` `sys.exit` fires (unchanged).\n\n### P3 — `terminus()` returns `(result, errors, fatal)` + `TerminusError` (current L327–353)\n\nAdopt the in-code TODO. `None` (not `\"\"`) on decode failure; return the 3-tuple; a named exception\nso a malformed response fails *at the call site with the real cause* instead of a `TypeError`\n(`\"\"[\"timeseries\"]`) far away.\n\n```\nrun_terminus(cmd) ── (output, errors, fatal) ─┐\n                                              json.loads(output)\n                            ┌──────────────────┴──────────────────┐\n                          ok                                   JSONDecodeError\n                           │                                       │\n                     result=parsed                     result=None; errors += output+exc\n                           └──────────────────┬──────────────────┘\n                                    errors != \"\" ?\n                          ┌──────────yes───────┴────────no─────────┐\n                 session-expired & retry?                     (fall through)\n                    │yes            │no\n              sleep+retry once   (kept)\n                                    └────────────► return (result, errors, fatal)\n                                                          │\n   caller:  result, errors, fatal = terminus(...)\n            if fatal or result is None:  raise TerminusError(command, errors)\n```\n\n- **New exception** `class TerminusError(RuntimeError)` — carries the command + captured stderr;\n  message the user sees: `Terminus command '<cmd>' failed: <errors>`. Triggered by: `fatal` True or\n  `result is None` at a call site that needs data. Caught: at top of `main()`'s per-site loop it is\n  logged as a per-site alert and the site is skipped (no whole-run abort); for org-level calls\n  (`org:site:list`, `self:info`) it aborts with a clear message. Tested: yes (integration).\n- **10 call sites** (current L487, 925, 1030, 1084, 1153, 1193, 1318, 2130, 2276, 3449) each become\n  `x, errors, fatal = terminus(...)`. Data-indexing sites (1084 `[\"sku\"]`, 487/1193 `[\"timeseries\"]`,\n  1318 `domains`, 3449 `site_team`, 1153 `envs`, 2276 `updates`, 2130 `audit`) check `fatal`/`None`\n  before indexing; the L925 `pprint` site just unpacks.\n- Shadow paths: `None` (decode fail) → `TerminusError`; valid-but-empty `{}`/`[]` → callers already\n  loop/`in`-check, now with an explicit \"empty response\" debug log so zero-row runs aren't silent;\n  upstream error → `fatal`/`errors` propagate.\n\n**Note:** `wp()`/`drush()` already return 3-tuples with `None`-on-decode + captured errors, so they\nare *not* changed by P3 (only their P6 docstrings are). `TerminusError` is terminus-only.\n\n### P4 — classify DNS outcomes into structured notices (current L1341–1407)\n\nDefinitive vs transient must be distinguished, and both must reach the report (not console-only).\n\n**Extraction for testability + observability:** `classify_hostname_dns(hostname, cloudflare_enabled,\ncf_v4_nets, cf_v6_nets) -> (points_at_cloudflare: int, points_elsewhere: int, notices: list, transient: bool)`.\n`main()` calls it, adds the returned notices via `sc.add_notice(...)`, and only emits the existing\n`ATTENTION: … is not in DNS` alert when both counts are 0 **and** `transient` is False.\n\n```\nresolve(host, A) / resolve(host, AAAA)\n  ├─ answers ──────► classify each IP: Cloudflare net? → points_at_cloudflare++ else points_elsewhere++\n  ├─ NXDOMAIN / NoAnswer      ► DEFINITIVE : notice(type=alert,   \"<host> is not in DNS\")\n  └─ Timeout / NoNameservers  ► TRANSIENT  : notice(type=warning, \"DNS lookup for <host> failed\n                                             (transient) — rerun the report\"); transient=True\nafter both records (unchanged aggregation):\n  if points_at_cloudflare==0 and points_elsewhere==0 and not transient:\n        not_in_dns.append(host)          # KEEP: the single aggregated \"not in DNS\" notice\n  if transient:  do NOT append to not_in_dns, do NOT claim \"not in DNS\"\n```\n**Aggregation preserved.** The existing code emits ONE aggregated `not_in_dns` notice over all hosts\n(current L1592–1611) — that notice is **unchanged**. P4 does not switch to per-host \"not in DNS\"\nnotices; it only (a) keeps hosts out of `not_in_dns` when the failure was transient, and (b) adds\n*diagnostic* notices: a `warning` transient notice per transiently-failing host, and (optionally) an\n`info` note for definitive per-host failures — via `sc.add_notice()`. This keeps the offline golden\nbyte-identical (no `not_in_dns` hosts there) and does not restructure the aggregated notice.\nAlso fixes the incidental missing `style=\"red\"` on the AAAA `NoAnswer` console line.\nShadow paths: both records NXDOMAIN → host lands in `not_in_dns` (as today); A transient + AAAA\nanswer → resolved, no transient notice; resolver import/None → treated as transient.\n\n### P5 — deferred\nNo change. Keep the problems-doc entry; the `--all` summary and SMTP send remain as-is.\n\n### P6 — correct wrapper docstrings/annotations (current L356, 370, 427, 442)\n`wp()`, `wp_eval()`, `drush()`, `drush_php_script()` are annotated `-> (Any, str)` / `-> (str, str)`\nbut return 3-tuples `(result, errors, fatal)`. Correct each annotation to the real 3-tuple and fix\n`wp()`'s docstring (it says \"wp eval / return JSON\" but runs a generic `wp` command). No runtime\nchange; `tests/integration/test_wrappers.py` already pins the truth and stays green.\n\n### P7 — correct misleading comment (current L3720)\n`plt.close(fig)  # needed to free up memory when sc.options.all_sites is True` → the real option is\n`sc.options.all`. Comment-only.\n\n### P8 — pragmatic-subset relocation of U-M logic\n\n**8a. Email/SMTP → config (new keys; defaults reproduce current literals byte-for-byte).**\n```\n[Email]\n  from        = \"University of Michigan Webmaster Team <webmaster@umich.edu>\"\n  reply_to    = \"webmaster@umich.edu\"\n  bcc         = \"januside@go.mail.umich.edu, its-webmaster@go.mail.umich.edu\"   # for_real only\n  dry_run_to  = \"januside@go.mail.umich.edu\"        # joined with {smtp_username}@<dry_run_username_domain>\n  dry_run_username_domain = \"umich.edu\"             # domain appended to smtp_username in dry-run To\n  msgid_domain = \"webservices.umich.edu\"\n[SMTP]\n  host = \"smtp.mail.umich.edu\"\n  port = 465\n```\n- `make_msgid(domain=...)` at core L3587–3588 and `check/umich/sitelens.py` L207 read\n  `[Email].msgid_domain`.\n- MIME headers (core L3661–3671) read `[Email].from/reply_to/bcc/dry_run_to` +\n  `dry_run_username_domain`. **Preserve the exact `Reply-to` capitalization** (not RFC `Reply-To`) —\n  `EmailMessage` preserves header-name case, so reading from config reproduces the exact byte.\n- `smtp_login()` (L769–773) reads `[SMTP].host/port` (dormant — only called from commented send).\n- When a key is absent, the default IS the current literal → U-M output unchanged.\n- **Verification (no `.eml` golden exists today):** goldens are HTML (CID-normalized) + TXT only; the\n  `.eml`'s `Date:` (L3672, `datetime.now(UTC)`) is volatile, which is why there is no byte `.eml`\n  golden — so the moved MIME headers are currently **unguarded**. **Before P8a**, add a targeted\n  header-assertion test (`tests/e2e/test_eml_headers.py`) rendering the `.eml` and asserting the exact\n  `From` / `Reply-to` / `Bcc` / dry-run `To` / `Message-ID`-domain bytes (scrubbing only `Date:` and\n  the `make_msgid` CID left-hand side). Only then is \"byte-identical headers\" a checkable claim.\n\n**8b. Guard the fqdns-gated Cloudflare/doc-URL checks behind `[UMich].enabled` (in-place).** The WP\n`umich-cloudflare` check (L1665–1689 region) and the Drupal cloudflare-module checks (L2010–2043)\nare gated only by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) > 0`, so they emit U-M `node/5114`/`node/4242`\ndoc-URL notices on *any* institution. Wrap each in the existing\n`\"UMich\" in sc.config and … [\"enabled\"]` guard **in place**. This is NOT a package relocation — a\nclean relocation needs a new post-gather per-site hook seam because the existing `check` hook fires\nat L1293, before `fqdns_behind_cloudflare` (L1325/L1421) and the plugin/module data exist (deferred;\nsee NOT-in-scope). The `umich-oidc-login` / Hummingbird / Drupal user-agent notices carry U-M\nspecifics too but stay this round (NOT-in-scope) unless an in-place guard is trivially byte-identical.\n\n```\n[Email]/[SMTP] config ──default──► exact U-M literals (output unchanged)\ncore main() ─ headers/msgid/smtp ─► read config (+ header-assertion test as the guard)\ncore loop ─ fqdns-gated CF checks ─► wrapped in [UMich].enabled guard (silent on non-U-M)\n```\n\n**Riskiest to keep byte-identical:** the `.eml` MIME block + msgid domain; guarded by the new\nheader-assertion test.
