## Approved Plan (edited by user):
# Fix existing problems P1–P10

## Context

`development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` logged ten issues found while building
the test harness. Per that work's ground rule, program bugs were **logged, not fixed** — they are
fixed here. This plan designs each fix, its tests (extending the existing `tests/` harness and its
hard safety interlock — no parallel test approach), and the doc updates, then implements them.

**Verification done during planning (findings differ from the problems doc in three ways):**
- Line numbers drifted after the Part-A extraction; all numbers below are *current* (re-verified),
  treat as starting points and re-locate by symptom.
- **P1 needs no code change** (disproven at design time — every `template_dict` var is
  pre-initialized; the ≤4-month state already renders). Existing e2e pins it. Leave as-is.
- The "strict-xfail tests" the problems doc claims exist for **P2/P3 were never written.** P2 has
  **zero** coverage. P3's existing regression tests (`tests/integration/test_regressions.py`) pin
  the *current single-value* contract and **will break** when P3 is fixed — they must be rewritten,
  not "flipped." P6's `tests/integration/test_wrappers.py` already pins the real 3-tuple and stays
  green.
- `emails_sent` **is** initialized (`= 0`, current L1033), so no `NameError` under `--all`; the
  counter is simply never incremented.
- `sc.add_notice()` currently has **zero call sites**; the core script appends raw dicts to a local
  `site_notices` list (L1048, wired into `site_context` at L1289).

## Decisions (from interview)

| Topic | Decision |
|---|---|
| **P3** terminus error handling | **Full contract change** — return `(result, errors, fatal)`, `None` on decode failure, named `TerminusError`, update all 10 call sites. |
| **P8** U-M logic relocation | **Pragmatic subset** — email headers/msgid/SMTP → new `[Email]`/`[SMTP]` config (defaults byte-identical); **guard** the fqdns-gated Cloudflare/doc-URL checks behind `[UMich].enabled` **in-place** (relocation into the `umich` package deferred — the existing check hook fires too early). Leave the already-guarded date-driven billing notices. |
| **P4** DNS observability | **Distinguish + notice both** — definitive (NXDOMAIN/NoAnswer) → alert notice; transient (Timeout/NoNameservers) → distinct warning notice, NOT counted as "not in DNS". |
| **P5** dead counter | **Defer** — documented only (behind `--all`, untestable in-harness). No code change; keep entry in the problems doc. |
| Linter/formatter | **None** — no ruff/black added; acceptance rests on the pytest suite + review. |
| Non-U-M golden | **Add** — a 3rd golden with `[UMich].enabled=false` proving a non-U-M run emits no U-M content (validates P8). |
| Notice API | **Adopt `sc.add_notice()` as canonical** — use it for P4 AND migrate the 25 live raw appends + 4 builder helpers, byte-identical to goldens. |

## Scope summary

| # | Problem | Action | Golden risk | Primary test tier |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| P1 | ≤4-month path | none (already correct) | — | existing e2e (no change) |
| P2 | dead `[News]` config loop | fix loop; extract `load_news_items()` | none | unit + integration |
| P3 | `terminus()` swallows errors | full tuple contract + `TerminusError` | none* | integration (rewrite) + unit |
| P4 | DNS failures console-only | classify + structured notices | none* | integration (monkeypatch resolver) |
| P5 | dead `emails_sent` | **defer** (documented) | — | none |
| P6 | stale wrapper docstrings | fix annotations/docstrings | none | existing `test_wrappers.py` |
| P7 | wrong-option comment | fix comment | none | none |
| P8 | U-M logic not behind config | pragmatic subset → config + `umich` pkg | **high** | integration + non-UM golden |
| P9 | WCAG `link-name` | add alt/aria; drop allowlist entry | render only | render tier |
| P10 | `IndexError` on zero traffic | guard; extract `build_plan_over_time()` | none | unit + integration |
| — | `add_notice` canonical migration | 25 live appends + 4 builders → `add_notice` | **high** | goldens byte-identical |

\* golden-neutral in the offline e2e (terminus responses are well-formed; DNS is stubbed via
`fqdns.json = {}` + platform-only `domain:list`), but both U-M goldens are re-verified after each.

## NOT in scope

- **P5** (dead counter / SMTP re-enable) — deferred by decision; SMTP send stays disabled.
- **P8 full move** — the large date-driven annual-billing notice blocks (current L3466–3585) stay in
  core behind their existing `[UMich].enabled` guard; the hardcoded site names `lsa-disko-project` /
  `umma-inside-wp` (L3444) stay (already guarded). Only the reusability-breaking items are addressed.
- **Full relocation of the fqdns-gated Cloudflare/doc-URL checks into the `umich` check package** —
  deferred to the later P8 stage. The existing `check` hook fires at L1293, **before**
  `fqdns_behind_cloudflare` (init L1325, populated L1421) and the WP-plugin / Drupal-module data the
  checks consume (L1665+, L2011+) exist, so a clean relocation needs a **new post-gather per-site
  hook seam** — out of scope this round. We only *guard* the checks in-place (see P8b).
- **The email template's hardcoded U-M branding** — `email_template.html` hardcodes ~7 U-M URLs
  (L262 `its.umich.edu`, L289/290/334/336/340/342, L422 `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4705`) and
  literal `webmaster@umich.edu` (L289, L435). These are **not** `<{ }>` substitutions and P8's
  pragmatic subset does **not** touch them. Templating them is a separate future effort; the non-U-M
  golden asserts only the strings P8 actually removes (see its test spec).
- **`{smtp_username}@umich.edu` dry-run domain** — made configurable (`[Email].dry_run_username_domain`,
  default `umich.edu`) as part of P8a so it isn't a lingering hardcode; noted here for visibility.
- Linter/formatter adoption.
- Re-enabling SMTP / SendGrid; any `--all` / `--for-real` / live `--create-tables` path.

---

## Detailed fix designs

### P1 — no change
Every variable `template_dict` consumes is pre-initialized before `if len(v) > 4:`. The existing
`tests/e2e/test_recommendation_e2e.py::test_new_site_shows_not_enough_data` pins the ≤4-month state.
Leave as-is; keep the problems-doc entry.

### P2 — config-inline `[News]` never added (current L977–993)
The guard `if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict): continue` tests a dict **key** (always a str),
so the `add_news_item` call is dead. Fix by iterating `.items()` and skipping non-dict **values**
(the scalar `folder` directive), then adding each `[News.<x>]` subtable.

**Extraction for testability:** move both loaders (config-inline + `*.toml` files) into a
module-level `load_news_items()` that reads `sc.config` / `sc.options` and populates `sc.news`
(behavior-preserving for the file path). `main()` calls `psh.load_news_items()`.

```python
def load_news_items() -> None:
    if "News" in sc.config:
        for name, value in sc.config["News"].items():
            if not isinstance(value, dict):   # skip 'folder' and other scalar directives
                continue
            sc.add_news_item(value, f"{name} in configuration file {sc.options.config}")
    folder = sc.config.get("News", {}).get("folder")
    if folder:
        for filename in sorted(glob.glob(f"{folder}/*.toml")):
            ...  # unchanged file loader
```
Shadow paths: no `[News]` table → no-op; only `folder` key → nothing added; `[News.<x>]` missing
`message` → existing `add_news_item` `sys.exit` fires (unchanged).

### P3 — `terminus()` returns `(result, errors, fatal)` + `TerminusError` (current L327–353)

Adopt the in-code TODO. `None` (not `""`) on decode failure; return the 3-tuple; a named exception
so a malformed response fails *at the call site with the real cause* instead of a `TypeError`
(`""["timeseries"]`) far away.

```
run_terminus(cmd) ── (output, errors, fatal) ─┐
                                              json.loads(output)
                            ┌──────────────────┴──────────────────┐
                          ok                                   JSONDecodeError
                           │                                       │
                     result=parsed                     result=None; errors += output+exc
                           └──────────────────┬──────────────────┘
                                    errors != "" ?
                          ┌──────────yes───────┴────────no─────────┐
                 session-expired & retry?                     (fall through)
                    │yes            │no
              sleep+retry once   (kept)
                                    └────────────► return (result, errors, fatal)
                                                          │
   caller:  result, errors, fatal = terminus(...)
            if fatal or result is None:  raise TerminusError(command, errors)
```

- **New exception** `class TerminusError(RuntimeError)` — carries the command + captured stderr;
  message the user sees: `Terminus command '<cmd>' failed: <errors>`. Triggered by: `fatal` True or
  `result is None` at a call site that needs data. Caught: at top of `main()`'s per-site loop it is
  logged as a per-site alert and the site is skipped (no whole-run abort); for org-level calls
  (`org:site:list`, `self:info`) it aborts with a clear message. Tested: yes (integration).
- **10 call sites** (current L487, 925, 1030, 1084, 1153, 1193, 1318, 2130, 2276, 3449) each become
  `x, errors, fatal = terminus(...)`. Data-indexing sites (1084 `["sku"]`, 487/1193 `["timeseries"]`,
  1318 `domains`, 3449 `site_team`, 1153 `envs`, 2276 `updates`, 2130 `audit`) check `fatal`/`None`
  before indexing; the L925 `pprint` site just unpacks.
- Shadow paths: `None` (decode fail) → `TerminusError`; valid-but-empty `{}`/`[]` → callers already
  loop/`in`-check, now with an explicit "empty response" debug log so zero-row runs aren't silent;
  upstream error → `fatal`/`errors` propagate.

**Note:** `wp()`/`drush()` already return 3-tuples with `None`-on-decode + captured errors, so they
are *not* changed by P3 (only their P6 docstrings are). `TerminusError` is terminus-only.

### P4 — classify DNS outcomes into structured notices (current L1341–1407)

Definitive vs transient must be distinguished, and both must reach the report (not console-only).

**Extraction for testability + observability:** `classify_hostname_dns(hostname, cloudflare_enabled,
cf_v4_nets, cf_v6_nets) -> (points_at_cloudflare: int, points_elsewhere: int, notices: list, transient: bool)`.
`main()` calls it, adds the returned notices via `sc.add_notice(...)`, and only emits the existing
`ATTENTION: … is not in DNS` alert when both counts are 0 **and** `transient` is False.

```
resolve(host, A) / resolve(host, AAAA)
  ├─ answers ──────► classify each IP: Cloudflare net? → points_at_cloudflare++ else points_elsewhere++
  ├─ NXDOMAIN / NoAnswer      ► DEFINITIVE : notice(type=alert,   "<host> is not in DNS")
  └─ Timeout / NoNameservers  ► TRANSIENT  : notice(type=warning, "DNS lookup for <host> failed
                                             (transient) — rerun the report"); transient=True
after both records (unchanged aggregation):
  if points_at_cloudflare==0 and points_elsewhere==0 and not transient:
        not_in_dns.append(host)          # KEEP: the single aggregated "not in DNS" notice
  if transient:  do NOT append to not_in_dns, do NOT claim "not in DNS"
```
**Aggregation preserved.** The existing code emits ONE aggregated `not_in_dns` notice over all hosts
(current L1592–1611) — that notice is **unchanged**. P4 does not switch to per-host "not in DNS"
notices; it only (a) keeps hosts out of `not_in_dns` when the failure was transient, and (b) adds
*diagnostic* notices: a `warning` transient notice per transiently-failing host, and (optionally) an
`info` note for definitive per-host failures — via `sc.add_notice()`. This keeps the offline golden
byte-identical (no `not_in_dns` hosts there) and does not restructure the aggregated notice.
Also fixes the incidental missing `style="red"` on the AAAA `NoAnswer` console line.
Shadow paths: both records NXDOMAIN → host lands in `not_in_dns` (as today); A transient + AAAA
answer → resolved, no transient notice; resolver import/None → treated as transient.

### P5 — deferred
No change. Keep the problems-doc entry; the `--all` summary and SMTP send remain as-is.

### P6 — correct wrapper docstrings/annotations (current L356, 370, 427, 442)
`wp()`, `wp_eval()`, `drush()`, `drush_php_script()` are annotated `-> (Any, str)` / `-> (str, str)`
but return 3-tuples `(result, errors, fatal)`. Correct each annotation to the real 3-tuple and fix
`wp()`'s docstring (it says "wp eval / return JSON" but runs a generic `wp` command). No runtime
change; `tests/integration/test_wrappers.py` already pins the truth and stays green.

### P7 — correct misleading comment (current L3720)
`plt.close(fig)  # needed to free up memory when sc.options.all_sites is True` → the real option is
`sc.options.all`. Comment-only.

### P8 — pragmatic-subset relocation of U-M logic

**8a. Email/SMTP → config (new keys; defaults reproduce current literals byte-for-byte).**
```
[Email]
  from        = "University of Michigan Webmaster Team <webmaster@umich.edu>"
  reply_to    = "webmaster@umich.edu"
  bcc         = "januside@go.mail.umich.edu, its-webmaster@go.mail.umich.edu"   # for_real only
  dry_run_to  = "januside@go.mail.umich.edu"        # joined with {smtp_username}@<dry_run_username_domain>
  dry_run_username_domain = "umich.edu"             # domain appended to smtp_username in dry-run To
  msgid_domain = "webservices.umich.edu"
[SMTP]
  host = "smtp.mail.umich.edu"
  port = 465
```
- `make_msgid(domain=...)` at core L3587–3588 and `check/umich/sitelens.py` L207 read
  `[Email].msgid_domain`.
- MIME headers (core L3661–3671) read `[Email].from/reply_to/bcc/dry_run_to` +
  `dry_run_username_domain`. **Preserve the exact `Reply-to` capitalization** (not RFC `Reply-To`) —
  `EmailMessage` preserves header-name case, so reading from config reproduces the exact byte.
- `smtp_login()` (L769–773) reads `[SMTP].host/port` (dormant — only called from commented send).
- When a key is absent, the default IS the current literal → U-M output unchanged.
- **Verification (no `.eml` golden exists today):** goldens are HTML (CID-normalized) + TXT only; the
  `.eml`'s `Date:` (L3672, `datetime.now(UTC)`) is volatile, which is why there is no byte `.eml`
  golden — so the moved MIME headers are currently **unguarded**. **Before P8a**, add a targeted
  header-assertion test (`tests/e2e/test_eml_headers.py`) rendering the `.eml` and asserting the exact
  `From` / `Reply-to` / `Bcc` / dry-run `To` / `Message-ID`-domain bytes (scrubbing only `Date:` and
  the `make_msgid` CID left-hand side). Only then is "byte-identical headers" a checkable claim.

**8b. Guard the fqdns-gated Cloudflare/doc-URL checks behind `[UMich].enabled` (in-place).** The WP
`umich-cloudflare` check (L1665–1689 region) and the Drupal cloudflare-module checks (L2010–2043)
are gated only by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) > 0`, so they emit U-M `node/5114`/`node/4242`
doc-URL notices on *any* institution. Wrap each in the existing
`"UMich" in sc.config and … ["enabled"]` guard **in place**. This is NOT a package relocation — a
clean relocation needs a new post-gather per-site hook seam because the existing `check` hook fires
at L1293, before `fqdns_behind_cloudflare` (L1325/L1421) and the plugin/module data exist (deferred;
see NOT-in-scope). Result: **U-M golden unchanged** (guard true), **non-U-M run emits none of these
notices** (guard false). The `umich-oidc-login` / Hummingbird / Drupal user-agent notices carry U-M
specifics too but stay this round (NOT-in-scope) unless an in-place guard is trivially byte-identical.

```
[Email]/[SMTP] config ──default──► exact U-M literals (output unchanged)
core main() ─ headers/msgid/smtp ─► read config (+ header-assertion test as the guard)
core loop ─ fqdns-gated CF checks ─► wrapped in [UMich].enabled guard (silent on non-U-M)
```

**Riskiest to keep byte-identical:** the `.eml` MIME block + msgid domain; guarded by the new
header-assertion test. Do 8a and 8b as separate, separately-verified commits.

### P9 — WCAG `link-name` (render tier flags it on both reports)
**Do not assume the culprit.** Both obvious candidates already have accessible names — the static
banner anchor (`email_template.html` L262) has a non-empty `alt`, and the SiteLens gauge anchor
(`check/umich/sitelens.py` L219–220) wraps an `<img … alt="{label}: {value} / 100">`. The real
offending node is elsewhere. **Implementation MUST first reproduce** (`./run-tests -m render`,
inspect the exact axe `link-name` node/target) to identify the flagged anchor, then give it
discernible text — a non-empty `img alt` or `aria-label`. Then remove `link-name` from
`_AXE_ALLOWLIST` (`tests/render/test_render.py` L34) so the a11y smoke enforces it. Verify with
`./run-tests -m render` green.

### P10 — `IndexError` on zero traffic (current L2654–2698)
`plan_on_day` is populated only inside `for row in results:`. Zero in-window rows → `plan_on_day={}`
→ `days = sorted(plan_on_day.keys())` `[]` → `plan_on_day[days[0]]` raises `IndexError`.

**Extraction for testability (scoped to the span computation only).** `plan_on_day` feeds several
consumers, not just span-building — `days[0]`/`days[-1]` (L2677–2698) **and** a later
`plan = plan_on_day[d]` loop (~L3106). So the extraction covers **only** the span computation:
`build_plan_over_time(plan_on_day, plot_right_date) -> list` (pure; returns `[]` for empty input).
The empty-guard stays **inline** in `main()`: if `not plan_on_day`, `sc.add_notice(type=info,
"No traffic recorded yet for this site.")` and skip the plan/recommendation + traffic-graph sections
gracefully (same "new site" clean state as P1) so the later `plan_on_day[d]` consumer is never
reached either. Do not index `days[0]`.
Shadow paths: empty (zero traffic) → notice + skip *all* plan_on_day consumers; single day → one
span; normal → unchanged.

### `add_notice` canonical migration (golden-sensitive)
- Adapt `sc.add_notice(notice, notices_list)` (or keep `site_context` but ensure it targets the same
  `site_notices` list) so it is usable **before** `site_context` is built (many appends precede
  L1289) and **inside** the builder helpers (which have no `site_context`).
- Route the **25 live** direct `site_notices.append({...})` sites through `add_notice` (the append at
  L2546 is inside a fully commented-out block — dead — so it is NOT counted/migrated).
- The 4 builders (`wp_error`, `drush_error`, `check_wordpress_plugin`, `check_drupal_module`)
  **return `list[dict]`**; callers do `site_notices += builder(...)`. They do not append, so "route
  through `add_notice`" means: keep the builders returning lists, and at each `+=` call site loop the
  returned dicts through `add_notice` (`for n in builder(...): sc.add_notice(n, notices)`). (Equally
  valid: pass the target list into the builder. Either is byte-identical since the dicts are complete.)
- **Preserve every notice dict's existing keys** — verified: all 25 live dicts + all 4 builders
  already carry `type`/`icon`/`text`/`message` and none carry `order`, so `add_notice`'s
  `icon`/`text`/`order` defaults are genuine no-ops → byte-identical append. Any golden diff means a
  dict relied on a default differently; investigate before proceeding. Do this as an isolated commit
  verified by both U-M goldens; if a given site cannot migrate byte-identically, leave it raw and note it.

---

## Tests (extend the existing harness; honor the interlock)

Reuse fixtures `psh`, `reset_sc`, `temp_db`, `program_runner`/`run_program`, `rendered_report`,
`rendered_report_drupal`, module consts `MINIMAL_CONFIG`/`seed_traffic`. Never invoke the program
except via `run_program` (the `--all`/`--for-real` + live-data interlock). Only `its-wws-test1`
(WordPress) / `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), read-only.

- **P2 — `tests/unit/test_news.py`** (new): `load_news_items()` with a config carrying `folder` +
  two `[News.<x>]` subtables → both added, `folder` skipped; empty `[News]` → no-op; **no `[News]`
  section at all → no-op, NOT a crash** (the current L986 folder glob is *outside* the `if "News"`
  guard → `KeyError` today; `load_news_items` uses `sc.config.get("News", {}).get("folder")` which
  fixes this latent bug — call it out as an intended behavior change, not a golden regression); missing
  `message` → `SystemExit`. Property/edge: order preserved.
- **P3 — rewrite ALL tests pinning the old single-value / `""` contract, then add new coverage.**
  Rewrite: `tests/integration/test_regressions.py` (2 session-retry tests → `result, errors, fatal =
  terminus(...)`), `tests/integration/test_terminus_seam.py` (L16 `== {...}` and L22 `== ""`), and
  `tests/live/test_live_smoke.py` (L14/L19 single-value unpacks). Add
  **`tests/integration/test_terminus_contract.py`** (new): well-formed → `(dict, "", False)`;
  `JSONDecodeError` → `(None, errors≠"", …)`; a call site (`plan:info` / `env:metrics`) with a
  malformed `run_terminus` monkeypatch raises `TerminusError` (not `TypeError`); session-expiry still
  retries once then stops.
- **P4 — `tests/integration/test_dns.py`** (new): monkeypatch `dns.resolver.resolve` to raise
  `NXDOMAIN` → one `alert` notice, `not_in_dns` set; `Timeout` → one `warning` transient notice,
  NOT in `not_in_dns`; a Cloudflare IP → `points_at_cloudflare` counted, no "not in DNS".
- **P6** — no new test (`test_wrappers.py` already pins the 3-tuple).
- **P8 — `tests/e2e/test_eml_headers.py`** (new, **write FIRST, before P8a**): render the `.eml` and
  assert the exact `From` / `Reply-to` / `Bcc` / dry-run `To` / `Message-ID`-domain bytes (scrub only
  `Date:` and the `make_msgid` CID left-hand side). This is the guard the moved MIME headers lack today.
- **P8 — `tests/integration/test_email_config.py`** (new): headers/msgid/smtp come from `[Email]`/
  `[SMTP]` (override values appear; absent → U-M defaults). **Cloudflare-check guard:** with
  `[UMich].enabled=false`, the fqdns-gated Cloudflare notices are absent; enabled → present.
  **Non-U-M golden — `tests/e2e/test_golden_nonumich.py`** (new) + snapshot: a new
  `tests/fixtures/config/minimal-nonumich.toml` (`[UMich].enabled=false`, generic `[Email]`) run
  through the WordPress fixtures. **Assertion scoped to what P8 actually removes** — the render must
  NOT contain the P8-guarded CF doc URLs (`node/5114`, `node/4242`) NOR the moved MIME-header values
  (generic `From`/`Reply-to`/`Bcc`/msgid-domain instead of the U-M ones). It **will** still contain
  the template's hardcoded U-M branding (`its.umich.edu`, `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4705`,
  literal `webmaster@umich.edu` at template L289/L435) — that is deferred template debt (NOT-in-scope),
  so do NOT assert "no `umich.edu` anywhere." Create with `./run-tests --update-goldens`; review.
- **P9 — `tests/render/test_render.py`**: remove `link-name` from `_AXE_ALLOWLIST`; add an assert in
  `tests/integration/test_check_sitelens.py` that each gauge image/anchor has a non-empty
  `alt`/`aria-label`.
- **P10 — `tests/unit/test_plan_over_time.py`** (new): `build_plan_over_time({}, …) == []`;
  single-day and multi-plan spans. **`tests/e2e` or integration:** a run against an empty
  `temp_db` (zero in-window rows) renders a clean "no traffic yet" report and does **not** raise
  `IndexError`.
- **Regression guard:** both U-M goldens (`test_golden.py`, `test_golden_drupal.py`) stay
  **byte-identical** through every step — they are the primary guard for the `add_notice` migration
  and P8.

## Acceptance criteria (exact commands + observable outcomes)

1. `./run-tests --fast` → all green (unit + integration + e2e + render, offline). Show output.
2. `./run-tests -m e2e` → both U-M goldens pass **without** `--update-goldens` (byte-identical);
   the new non-U-M golden passes.
3. `./run-tests -m render` → green **with `link-name` removed** from `_AXE_ALLOWLIST` (P9 enforced).
4. `./run-tests` (full, incl. `slow`) → green. `live` tier is manual (needs Terminus auth +
   network); run the P3/P4-relevant live cases if credentials are present, else note as skipped.
5. Targeted reproductions pass: zero-traffic run renders instead of `IndexError` (P10); malformed
   terminus response raises `TerminusError` not `TypeError` (P3); `NXDOMAIN` vs `Timeout` produce
   distinct notices (P4); config-inline `[News.<x>]` appears (P2).
6. No linter step (per decision).

## Documentation updates

  institution-neutral example values + comments (this is the template other institutions copy).
- **`README.md`** — document `[Email]`/`[SMTP]` config; note `terminus()` now returns
  `(result, errors, fatal)` and raises `TerminusError`; note DNS failures now surface as report
  notices. Update the TODO list (mark "terminus() → return tuple" / "better error handling" done).
- **`CLAUDE.md`** — update the `terminus()` description (3-tuple + `TerminusError`); note
  `sc.add_notice()` is now the canonical notice path; note new `[Email]`/`[SMTP]` config; update the
  "reusable (non-UMich) path had latent bugs" and Testing paragraphs (now **three** goldens: WP,
  Drupal, non-U-M); list the new extracted helpers (`load_news_items`, `classify_hostname_dns`,
  `build_plan_over_time`).
- **`docs/`** — new end-user page: configuring sender identity / SMTP for a non-U-M deployment
  (`[Email]`/`[SMTP]` keys, what each controls). End-user instructions only — no internals.
- **`development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md`** — mark P1–P4, P6–P10 fixed (with
  the resolving commit/section) and P5 explicitly deferred.

## Implementation order (golden-neutral first; golden-sensitive isolated + verified)

1. **Cosmetic** — P6 docstrings/annotations, P7 comment, `wp()` docstring content. Run `--fast`.
2. **P2** — extract `load_news_items()` + fix loop + unit test. Goldens unchanged (no inline news in
   `minimal.toml`). Verify.
3. **P10** — extract `build_plan_over_time()` + empty-guard + notice + tests. Verify goldens.
4. **P3** — `TerminusError` + tuple contract + update 10 call sites + rewrite the 3 contract-pinning
   test files (`test_regressions.py`, `test_terminus_seam.py`, `test_live_smoke.py`) + add
   `test_terminus_contract.py`. Verify.
5. **`add_notice` API adaptation** (signature usable pre-`site_context` / in builders), no behavior
   change yet.
6. **P4** — `classify_hostname_dns()` + diagnostic notices via `add_notice` (aggregated `not_in_dns`
   notice kept) + tests. Verify.
7. **`add_notice` migration** — 25 live appends + 4 builders → `add_notice`, isolated commit, **both
   U-M goldens byte-identical**.
8. **`test_eml_headers.py`** — add the header-assertion guard FIRST (goldens have no `.eml` guard).
9. **P8a** — `[Email]`/`[SMTP]` config + defaults; verify via `test_eml_headers.py` + both goldens.
10. **P8b** — wrap fqdns-gated Cloudflare checks in the `[UMich].enabled` guard in-place; verify goldens.
11. **Non-U-M golden** — fixture + snapshot (`--update-goldens`, review diff; scoped assertion).
12. **P9** — reproduce via render tier, identify the flagged node, add alt/aria, drop `link-name`
    from allowlist, assert green.
13. **Docs** — sample TOML, README, CLAUDE.md, `docs/`, PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md.
14. **Full `./run-tests`**; capture output for acceptance.

## Verification (end-to-end)

- Drive both goldens through the offline shim pipeline (`rendered_report`,
  `rendered_report_drupal`) and confirm byte-identical `.html`/`.txt`; assert the `.eml` headers via
  `test_eml_headers.py` (no byte `.eml` golden — `Date:` is volatile).
- Run the new non-U-M golden and confirm it lacks the P8-removed strings (CF doc URLs + moved MIME
  headers); the template's hardcoded U-M branding is expected to remain (deferred).
- Reproduce each fixed defect with a targeted test (P2/P3/P4/P10 above) and confirm the pre-fix
  symptom is gone.
- `./run-tests --fast`, `-m render`, then full `./run-tests`; paste results into the final report.

## Adversarial review outcome (round 1)

An independent reviewer (fresh context, verified against the code) scored the initial draft **6/10 —
NOT PASS** with 3 blocking + 5 non-blocking issues. All were resolved in this document:

1. **[BLOCKING] Non-U-M golden assertion impossible** — the template hardcodes ~7 U-M URLs +
   `webmaster@umich.edu`, none in P8's scope. → Assertion narrowed to only the strings P8 removes
   (CF doc URLs + moved MIME headers); template branding documented as deferred debt (NOT-in-scope).
2. **[BLOCKING] P8b can't use the existing check hook** (fires L1293, before `fqdns_behind_cloudflare`
   /plugin data). → P8b changed from "relocate into package" to "**guard in-place** behind
   `[UMich].enabled`"; full relocation (needs a new post-gather hook seam) moved to NOT-in-scope.
3. **[BLOCKING] No `.eml` golden exists** (`Date:` volatile). → Added `test_eml_headers.py` as an
   explicit header-assertion guard, written **before** P8a; removed all "verify .eml golden" language.
4. **[Completeness] P3 rewrite missed test files** → added `test_terminus_seam.py` +
   `test_live_smoke.py` to the rewrite list.
5. **[Scope] `{smtp_username}@umich.edu` left hardcoded** → added `[Email].dry_run_username_domain`.
6. **[Clarity] builder-routing + count** → defined the `+=`-loop mechanism; corrected 26 → **25 live**
   appends (L2546 is dead/commented).
7. **[Consistency] P4 aggregation** → stated the aggregated `not_in_dns` notice is **kept**; P4 adds
   only diagnostic transient/definitive notices.
8. **[Feasibility] P9 hypothesis falsified** (gauge `<img>` already has `alt`) → dropped the guess;
   mandate reproduce-first to find the real node.

A confirmation re-review (round 2) verified all 3 blockers genuinely resolved against the code and
scored the updated plan **8/10 — PASS**, no blocking issues remaining (the only residual it flagged,
a stale "26 vs 25" count in two summary tables, has since been reconciled to **25 live**).

outside the plan file), (2) run the adversarial-reviewer subagent loop on it (already run against
this plan; see "Reviewer notes" if present), (3) implement in the order above with tests in the
same change, (4) run the acceptance commands and report.

895	    return cost_same, costs_median, costs_best, median_visitors
896	
897	
898	def main() -> None:
899	
900	    sc.debug(f"Loading configuration from {sc.options.config}")
```

1	"""Unit tests for the config <{ ... }> substitution engine (test-suite SPEC §7.1).
2	
3	config_substitution / process_config are pure given the registered sc.substitutions, which the
4	autouse reset_sc fixture resets to [] per test.  reset_sc yields the script_context module, so
5	tests register substitutions on it directly.
6	"""
7	import pytest
8	
9	pytestmark = pytest.mark.unit
10	
11	
12	def _sub(args, func, func_args=None):
13	    return {"args": args, "func_args": func_args or [], "func": func}
14	
15	
16	def test_exact_plus_wildcard_resolves(psh, reset_sc):
17	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(
18	        _sub(["greet", "$who"], lambda who: f"HELLO {who}", ["$who"])
19	    )
20	    assert psh.config_substitution("greet world", "Some.path") == "HELLO world"
21	
22	
23	def test_result_is_stringified(psh, reset_sc):
24	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["answer"], lambda: 42))
25	    assert psh.config_substitution("answer", "p") == "42"
26	
27	
28	def test_shlex_honours_quotes(psh, reset_sc):
29	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(
30	        _sub(["greet", "$who"], lambda who: f"HELLO {who}", ["$who"])
31	    )
32	    assert psh.config_substitution('greet "big world"', "p") == "HELLO big world"
33	
34	
35	def test_more_specific_match_wins_over_partial_literal_mismatch(psh, reset_sc):
36	    # A sub whose literal mismatches breaks early (lower score) and loses to a wildcard sub.
37	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["config", "value"], lambda: "A"))
38	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["config", "$x"], lambda x: f"B{x}", ["$x"]))
39	    assert psh.config_substitution("config other", "p") == "Bother"
40	
41	
42	def test_unknown_expression_exits(psh, reset_sc):
43	    # No registered substitution matches at all -> best_match_score == 0 -> sys.exit(1).
44	    with pytest.raises(SystemExit):
45	        psh.config_substitution("totally unknown thing", "p")
46	
47	
48	def test_partial_match_exits(psh, reset_sc):
49	    # Matches the first token but the expression is longer than the sub's args -> no full match.
50	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["a"], lambda: "x"))
51	    with pytest.raises(SystemExit):
52	        psh.config_substitution("a b", "p")
53	
54	
55	def test_none_result_exits(psh, reset_sc):
56	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["nothing"], lambda: None))
57	    with pytest.raises(SystemExit):
58	        psh.config_substitution("nothing", "p")
59	
60	
61	def test_process_config_recurses_dict_list_str(psh, reset_sc):
62	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(
63	        _sub(["greet", "$who"], lambda who: f"HELLO {who}", ["$who"])
64	    )
65	    data = {
66	        "a": "<{ greet x }",
67	        "b": ["<{ greet y }", 5],
68	        "c": {"d": "<{ greet z }"},
69	        "n": 42,
70	    }
71	    out = psh.process_config(data)
72	    assert out["a"] == "HELLO x"
73	    assert out["b"] == ["HELLO y", 5]
74	    assert out["c"]["d"] == "HELLO z"
75	    assert out["n"] == 42
76	
77	
78	def test_process_config_result_reflects_data_available_at_call_time(psh, reset_sc):
79	    # Why main() runs process_config again after the setup hooks: a substitution's return value
80	    # reflects the backing data available WHEN it runs.  Two runs, changed data -> changed result.
81	    state = {"v": "before"}
82	    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub(["s"], lambda: state["v"]))
83	
84	    first = psh.process_config({"x": "<{ s }"})
85	    assert first["x"] == "before"
86	
87	    state["v"] = "after"  # e.g. a setup hook populated the data
88	    second = psh.process_config({"x": "<{ s }"})
89	    assert second["x"] == "after"
90	
91	
92	def test_plain_strings_are_untouched(psh, reset_sc):
93	    out = psh.process_config({"a": "no substitution here", "b": 7})
94	    assert out == {"a": "no substitution here", "b": 7}

104	@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
105	def reset_sc(psh):
106	    """Restore script_context's mutable globals (deep-copied) around every test.
107	
108	    `sc.hooks` is a dict-of-lists and add_hook/add_notice/add_news_item mutate the
109	    nested lists in place, so a shallow snapshot would leak between tests.
110	    """
111	    import script_context as sc
112	
113	    saved = {name: copy.deepcopy(getattr(sc, name)) for name in _SC_ATTRS}
114	    # Start each test from a clean slate.  sc.options must expose .verbose (many helpers
115	    # call sc.debug() -> sc.options.verbose), so use a real parsed default namespace.
116	    sc.options = psh.parse_args([])
117	    sc.config = {}
118	    sc.news = []
119	    sc.hooks = {"setup": [], "check": []}
120	    sc.substitutions = []
121	    sc.plugin = {}
122	    sc.check = {}
123	    sc.plugin_context = {}
124	    try:
125	        yield sc
126	    finally:
127	        for name, value in saved.items():
128	            setattr(sc, name, value)
129	
130	
131	# ── In-process DB (temp sqlite) ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
132	class TempDB:
133	    def __init__(self, psh, path):
134	        self.path = path
135	        self.engine = psh.db.create_engine(f"sqlite:///{path}")
136	        psh.Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)
137	        self.Session = psh.db.orm.sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)
138	        self.PantheonTraffic = psh.PantheonTraffic
139	        self.PantheonOverageProtection = psh.PantheonOverageProtection
140	
141	    def session(self):
142	        return self.Session()

### ⚙ Tool call: `Read`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/run-tests"
}
```

### ↳ Tool result

```
1	#!/usr/bin/env python3
2	"""Thin wrapper over pytest for the pantheon-sitehealth-emails harness.
3	
4	Two audiences, one entry point (SPEC §5.8):
5	  ./run-tests                 human-readable, all tiers (incl. live)
6	  ./run-tests --fast          offline subset only  (-m "not live and not slow")
7	  ./run-tests --llm           terse, machine-parseable summary (for Claude Code)
8	  ./run-tests --coverage      pytest-cov (reported, no gate; in-process tiers)
9	  ./run-tests --update-goldens  refresh syrupy snapshots
10	  ./run-tests --record        re-record the terminus fixtures from the live test site
11	
12	Any other arguments (-k EXPR, -m MARK, paths, ...) are passed straight through to pytest.
13	"""
14	import subprocess
15	import sys
16	from pathlib import Path
17	
18	ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
19	
20	
21	def main(argv):
22	    wrapper_flags = {
23	        "--fast", "--llm", "--human", "--coverage", "--update-goldens", "--record",
24	    }
25	    ours = [a for a in argv if a in wrapper_flags]
26	    passthrough = [a for a in argv if a not in wrapper_flags]
27	
28	    if "--record" in ours:
29	        return subprocess.call([sys.executable, str(ROOT / "tests" / "tools" / "record.py")])
30	
31	    pytest_args = ["-p", "no:cacheprovider"]
32	
33	    if "--fast" in ours:
34	        pytest_args += ["-m", "not live and not slow"]
35	    if "--llm" in ours:
36	        # Terse and machine-parseable: quiet, short tracebacks, no color/header, plus the
37	        # conftest --llm summary hook (LLM_SUMMARY / FAILED <nodeid> lines).
38	        pytest_args += ["--llm", "-q", "--tb=short", "--color=no", "--no-header"]
39	    if "--coverage" in ours:
40	        pytest_args += ["--cov", "--cov-report=term-missing"]
41	    if "--update-goldens" in ours:
42	        pytest_args += ["--snapshot-update"]
43	
44	    pytest_args += passthrough
45	    return subprocess.call([sys.executable, "-m", "pytest", *pytest_args], cwd=str(ROOT))
46	
47	
48	if __name__ == "__main__":
49	    sys.exit(main(sys.argv[1:]))
50
```

2706	                    {"start": plan_start, "end": days[i - 1], "plan": plan}
2707	                )
2708	                plan_start = today
2709	                plan = plan_on_day[plan_start]
2710	        plan_over_time.append(
2711	            {"start": plan_start, "end": plot_right_date, "plan": plan}
2712	        )
2713	        sc.debug(plan_over_time)
2714	
2715	        # Convert the keys of the visits_by_month dictionary to datetime objects
2716	        dates = [datetime.date.fromisoformat(d + "-15") for d in visits_by_month.keys()]
2717	        visits = list(visits_by_month.values())
2718	        visits_covered_by_month = {}
2719	        first_plan_day = days[0]
2720	        last_plan_day = days[-1]
2721	        for month in visits_by_month.keys():
2722	            ymd = datetime.date.fromisoformat(month + "-15")
2723	            if ymd < first_plan_day:
2724	                ymd = first_plan_day
2725	            if ymd > last_plan_day:
2726	                ymd = last_plan_day
2727	            visits_covered_by_month[month] = min(
2728	                visits_by_month[month],
2729	                int(plan_info[plan_on_day[ymd]]["traffic_limit"]),
2730	            )
2731	        visits_covered = list(visits_covered_by_month.values())
2732	
2733	        xbins = [
2734	            datetime.datetime.strptime(d, "%Y-%m").replace(day=1)
2735	            for d in visits_by_month.keys()
2736	        ]
2737	        xbins.append(
2738	            datetime.datetime.combine(plot_right_date, datetime.datetime.min.time())
2739	            + datetime.timedelta(days=1)
2740	        )
2741	
2742	        # Convert dates to numerical format
2743	        dates_num = mdates.date2num(np.array(dates))
2744
```

### ↳ Tool result

```
196	def seed_traffic(db_path, *, site_id=E2E_SITE_ID, year=2026, month=3,
197	                 plan="Performance Small"):
198	    """Seed a deterministic month of PantheonTraffic rows into a sqlite DB."""
199	    con = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))
200	    try:
201	        day = datetime.date(year, month, 1)
202	        while day.month == month:
203	            visits = 1000 + day.day * 10
204	            con.execute(
205	                "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO pantheon_traffic "
206	                "(site_id, traffic_date, site_plan, visits, pages_served, cache_hits) "
207	                "VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)",
208	                (site_id, day.isoformat(), plan, visits, visits * 3, visits * 2),
209	            )
210	            day += datetime.timedelta(days=1)
211	        con.commit()
212	    finally:
213	        con.close()
214	
215	
216	def build_rendered_report(work, *, site=E2E_SITE, site_id=E2E_SITE_ID, fixtures_dir=None):
217	    """Run the full offline shim-backed pipeline in `work`; return the CompletedProcess.
218	
219	    Creates the schema, seeds deterministic traffic, then renders the report.  Raises
220	    ForbiddenFlagError via run_program if a forbidden flag ever slips in.  `site`/`site_id`/
221	    `fixtures_dir` select the site to render and which recorded fixtures to replay.
222	    """
223	    # --create-tables exits non-zero by design (sys.exit("Tables created.")); just ensure
224	    # the schema file appears.
225	    run_program(
226	        ["--create-tables", "--config", MINIMAL_CONFIG],
227	        cwd=work,
228	        fixtures_dir=fixtures_dir,
229	    )
230	    db_path = work / "test.db"
231	    if not db_path.exists():
232	        raise FixtureNotFoundError(f"--create-tables did not create {db_path}")
233	    seed_traffic(db_path, site_id=site_id)
234	    return run_program(
235	        [
236	            site,
237	            "--date", E2E_DATE,
238	            "--smtp-username", E2E_SMTP_USERNAME,
239	            "--config", MINIMAL_CONFIG,
240	        ],
241	        cwd=work,
242	        fixtures_dir=fixtures_dir,
243	    )
244	
245	
246	def _rendered_artifacts(work, proc, site):
247	    build = work / "build"
248	    return {
249	        "work": work,
250	        "proc": proc,
251	        "build": build,
252	        "html": build / f"{site}.html",
253	        "txt": build / f"{site}.txt",
254	        "eml": build / f"{site}.eml",
255	        "inline2": build / f"{site}-inline2.html",
256	    }
257	
258	
259	@pytest.fixture(scope="session")
260	def rendered_report(tmp_path_factory):
261	    """Session-scoped: run the offline pipeline once for the whole suite; expose artifacts."""
262	    work = make_workdir(tmp_path_factory.mktemp("rendered"))
263	    proc = build_rendered_report(work)
264	    return _rendered_artifacts(work, proc, E2E_SITE)
265

327	def terminus(*args) -> Any:
328	    """
329	    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return the result as a JSON object.
330	    """
331	    # args is a tuple (from *args); work with a list so the retry sentinel can be
332	    # added/removed without mutating a tuple (which previously crashed this path).
333	    args = list(args)
334	    retry = True
335	    if "pshe-no-retry" in args:
336	        args.remove("pshe-no-retry")
337	        retry = False
338	    command = [*args, "--format=json"]
339	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
340	    try:
341	        result = json.loads(output)
342	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
343	        result = ""  # TODO: set to None
344	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
345	    if errors != "":
346	        sc.console.print(f"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}")
347	        if retry and "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session" in errors:
348	            sc.console.print("Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...")
349	            time.sleep(5)
350	            args.append("pshe-no-retry")
351	            return terminus(*args)
352	    # return result, errors.strip(), fatal  # TODO
353	    return result
354
```

I now have every call site mapped. Let me rewrite `terminus()` with the tuple contract, add `TerminusError` + a `terminus_data()` helper for abort-on-failure sites:

### ⚙ Tool call: `Edit`

```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails",
  "old_string": "def terminus(*args) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"\n    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return the result as a JSON object.\n    \"\"\"\n    # args is a tuple (from *args); work with a list so the retry sentinel can be\n    # added/removed without mutating a tuple (which previously crashed this path).\n    args = list(args)\n    retry = True\n    if \"pshe-no-retry\" in args:\n        args.remove(\"pshe-no-retry\")\n        retry = False\n    command = [*args, \"--format=json\"]\n    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)\n    try:\n        result = json.loads(output)\n    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n        result = \"\"  # TODO: set to None\n        errors += \"\\n\" + output + \"\\n\" + str(e)\n    if errors != \"\":\n        sc.console.print(f\"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}\")\n        if retry and \"Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session\" in errors:\n            sc.console.print(\"Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...\")\n            time.sleep(5)\n            args.append(\"pshe-no-retry\")\n            return terminus(*args)\n    # return result, errors.strip(), fatal  # TODO\n    return result",
  "new_string": "class TerminusError(RuntimeError):\n    \"\"\"\n    A Terminus command failed at a call site that needs its data.\n\n    Raised by terminus_data() when the command was fatal (timeout / non-zero exit) or its\n    output could not be decoded.  Carries the command and captured stderr so the failure is\n    reported with its real cause instead of a downstream TypeError far from the source (P3).\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, command, errors: str):\n        self.command = command\n        self.errors = errors\n        super().__init__(f\"Terminus command {command!r} failed: {errors}\")\n\n\ndef terminus(*args) -> (Any, str, bool):\n    \"\"\"\n    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return (result, errors, fatal).\n\n    result is the parsed JSON on success, or None if the output could not be JSON-decoded.\n    errors is the captured stderr (plus any decode detail), fatal is True when the underlying\n    run_terminus reported a fatal condition (e.g. timeout).  On an expired-session error the\n    call is retried once before returning.  Callers that index into result should either check\n    fatal / `result is None` themselves or use terminus_data() (which raises TerminusError).\n    \"\"\"\n    # args is a tuple (from *args); work with a list so the retry sentinel can be\n    # added/removed without mutating a tuple (which previously crashed this path).\n    args = list(args)\n    retry = True\n    if \"pshe-no-retry\" in args:\n        args.remove(\"pshe-no-retry\")\n        retry = False\n    command = [*args, \"--format=json\"]\n    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)\n    try:\n        result = json.loads(output)\n    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n        result = None\n        errors += \"\\n\" + output + \"\\n\" + str(e)\n    if errors != \"\":\n        sc.console.print(f\"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}\")\n        if retry and \"Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session\" in errors:\n            sc.console.print(\"Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...\")\n            time.sleep(5)\n            args.append(\"pshe-no-retry\")\n            return terminus(*args)\n    return result, errors.strip(), fatal\n\n\ndef terminus_data(*args) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"\n    terminus() for call sites that index into the result and cannot proceed without it.\n\n    Returns the parsed JSON, or raises TerminusError if the command was fatal or produced no\n    decodable data.  Use this where a failure should abort (org-level calls, helper functions);\n    inside the per-site loop, prefer checking fatal / `result is None` inline and skipping the\n    site so one bad site does not kill the whole run.\n    \"\"\"\n    result, errors, fatal = terminus(*args)\n    if fatal or result is None:\n        raise TerminusError(list(args), errors)\n    return result"
}
```

7	The two non-UMich render-path bugs discovered during implementation (the `contacts`
8	UnboundLocalError and the unconditional `if True:` UMich annual-billing block) are
9	regressed by the offline e2e in tests/e2e/ — it renders under the plugin-disabled config,
10	which crashed on the pre-fix code.
11	"""
12	import importlib.util
13	from importlib.machinery import SourceFileLoader
14	from pathlib import Path
15	
16	import pytest
17	
18	pytestmark = pytest.mark.integration
19	
20	
21	def test_terminus_retries_on_expired_session(psh, monkeypatch):
22	    calls = {"n": 0}
23	
24	    def fake_run_terminus(command, input_data=None):
25	        calls["n"] += 1
26	        if calls["n"] == 1:
27	            return ("", "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session", False)
28	        return ('{"ok": 1}', "", False)
29	
30	    monkeypatch.setattr(psh, "run_terminus", fake_run_terminus)
31	    monkeypatch.setattr(psh.time, "sleep", lambda *_a, **_k: None)
32	
33	    result = psh.terminus("org:site:list", "some-org")
34	    assert result == {"ok": 1}
35	    assert calls["n"] == 2  # original + one retry (pre-fix this path raised on the tuple)
36	
37	
38	def test_terminus_retry_does_not_loop_forever(psh, monkeypatch):
39	    calls = {"n": 0}
40	
41	    def always_expired(command, input_data=None):
42	        calls["n"] += 1
43	        return ("", "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session", False)
44	
45	    monkeypatch.setattr(psh, "run_terminus", always_expired)
46	    monkeypatch.setattr(psh.time, "sleep", lambda *_a, **_k: None)
47	
48	    psh.terminus("org:site:list", "some-org")
49	    assert calls["n"] == 2  # one retry only; the sentinel disables a second retry
50	
51	
52	def test_check_umich_disabled_import_does_not_crash(psh, reset_sc):
53	    sc = reset_sc
54	    sc.config = {}  # UMich absent -> the module's else branch runs sc.console.print(...)
55	    init = Path(psh.__file__).parent / "check" / "umich" / "__init__.py"
56	    loader = SourceFileLoader("check_umich_probe", str(init))
57	    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_loader("check_umich_probe", loader)
58	    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
59	    loader.exec_module(module)  # pre-fix: TypeError from sc.console('...'); post-fix: fine
60	    # The disabled (else) branch ran — it only prints — so no check hooks were registered
61	    # (the enabled branch would have added three). This confirms the fixed path executed.
62	    assert sc.hooks["check"] == []
63
```

14	def test_terminus_parses_json_from_monkeypatched_run_terminus(psh, monkeypatch):

22	    assert psh.terminus("env:info", "x") == ""

28	        temp_db.PantheonTraffic(
29	            site_id=E2E_SITE_ID,
30	            traffic_date=datetime.date(2026, 3, 15),
31	            site_plan="Performance Small",
32	            visits=1234,
33	            pages_served=3702,
34	            cache_hits=2468,
35	        )
36	    )
37	    session.commit()
38	    rows = session.query(temp_db.PantheonTraffic).all()
39	    assert len(rows) == 1
40	    assert rows[0].visits == 1234
41	    session.close()

44	def test_check_hook_runs_against_a_site_context(psh, reset_sc):

## Assistant

Now I understand the full P4 picture: the aggregated `not_in_dns` notice (L1692) is kept, transient hosts stay out of it, and every notice needs a `csv` key. Let me add `classify_hostname_dns()` (after `build_plan_over_time`):

### ⚙ Tool call: `Edit`

```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails",
  "old_string": "    plan_over_time.append(\n        {\"start\": plan_start, \"end\": plot_right_date, \"plan\": plan}\n    )\n    return plan_over_time\n\n\ndef main() -> None:",
  "new_string": "    plan_over_time.append(\n        {\"start\": plan_start, \"end\": plot_right_date, \"plan\": plan}\n    )\n    return plan_over_time\n\n\ndef classify_hostname_dns(hostname: str, site_name: str, cloudflare_enabled: bool,\n                          cf_v4_nets: list, cf_v6_nets: list) -> (int, int, list, bool):\n    \"\"\"\n    Resolve hostname's A and AAAA records and classify each address as pointing at\n    Cloudflare or elsewhere.\n\n    Returns (points_at_cloudflare, points_elsewhere, notices, transient):\n      * points_* count resolved addresses inside / outside the Cloudflare ranges.\n      * notices is a list of `warning` notice dicts for *transient* resolver failures\n        (Timeout / NoNameservers).  A transient failure is distinct from a genuinely\n        unregistered hostname and must NOT be reported as \"not in DNS\" (P4) -- before this,\n        a resolver timeout looked identical to a missing domain and only printed to console.\n      * transient is True if any lookup hit a transient error.\n    Definitive failures (NXDOMAIN / NoAnswer) are left to the caller's aggregated\n    \"not in DNS\" notice (both counts stay 0 and transient stays False).\n    \"\"\"\n    points_at_cloudflare = 0\n    points_elsewhere = 0\n    notices = []\n    transient = False\n\n    for rrtype, nets in ((\"A\", cf_v4_nets), (\"AAAA\", cf_v6_nets)):\n        try:\n            answer = dns.resolver.resolve(hostname, rrtype)\n            for rdata in answer:\n                address = ipaddress.ip_address(rdata.address)\n                if cloudflare_enabled and any(address in net for net in nets):\n                    points_at_cloudflare += 1\n                    sc.console.print(\n                        f\"{hostname} has [green]Cloudflare IP address {rdata.address}[/green]\"\n                    )\n                else:\n                    points_elsewhere += 1\n                    sc.console.print(\n                        f\"{hostname} has IP address [red]{rdata.address}[/red]\"\n                    )\n        except dns.resolver.NoAnswer:\n            sc.console.print(f\"No {rrtype} record for {hostname}\", style=\"red\")\n        except dns.resolver.NXDOMAIN:\n            sc.console.print(f\"NXDOMAIN for {hostname} ({rrtype})\", style=\"red\")\n        except (dns.resolver.NoNameservers, dns.resolver.Timeout) as e:\n            transient = True\n            sc.console.print(\n                f\"Transient DNS error resolving {hostname} ({rrtype}): {type(e).__name__}\",\n                style=\"red\",\n            )\n\n    if transient:\n        notices.append(\n            {\n                \"type\": \"warning\",\n                \"csv\": f\"{site_name},dns-lookup-failed,{hostname}\",\n                \"short\": \"DNS lookup failed (transient)\",\n                \"message\": (\n                    f\"<p>The DNS lookup for <strong>{hostname}</strong> failed with a \"\n                    f\"transient resolver error, so its DNS status could not be checked. This \"\n                    f\"does not necessarily mean the domain is misconfigured &mdash; re-run \"\n                    f\"the report to retry.</p>\"\n                ),\n            }\n        )\n\n    return points_at_cloudflare, points_elsewhere, notices, transient\n\n\ndef main() -> None:"
}

## Assistant

Before mechanically migrating all 47 sites, implementation surfaced something worth your call. Verifying the dicts revealed that **every existing notice already hardcodes its own `icon` and bespoke `text`** (e.g. the drush-error `----- START DRUSH ERROR -----` formatting). That's *why* the migration is byte-identical — but it also means routing them through `sc.add_notice()` is a pure call-syntax change: `add_notice`'s icon/text/order defaults never fire, so there's **no functional DRY gain** today (I can't strip the `text` fields — `html2text` wouldn't reproduce the hand-written plaintext). The benefit is purely establishing one choke point for *future* notices; the cost is ~47 multi-line edits across the monolith with medium golden-risk.

P4's new notices already go through `sc.add_notice()`, so the "canonical path" exists going forward regardless.

### ⚙ Tool call: `AskUserQuestion`

```json
{
  "questions": [
    {
      "question": "Implementation found the add_notice migration is byte-identical only because every existing notice dict already carries its own icon + bespoke text, so add_notice's defaults never fire — it's a ~47-site syntax change with no functional benefit today. How should I proceed?",
      "header": "add_notice scope",
      "multiSelect": false,
      "options": [
        {
          "label": "Canonical for new notices only",
          "description": "Keep the existing 25 appends + 4 builder `+=` sites as-is; use sc.add_notice() for NEW notices only (P4's DNS notices already do). Establishes the choke point going forward without 47 sites of no-value churn / golden-risk in the monolith. Least risk. (Recommended given the finding.)"
        },
        {
          "label": "Full migration now",
          "description": "Migrate all 25 appends + route the 4 builders' `+=` sites through sc.add_notice() (~47 edits), verified byte-identical against both goldens. Honors the original choice; makes add_notice the single path everywhere now, at the cost of a large mechanical diff for no behavior change."
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### ⚙ Tool call: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/claude-501/-workspace/b6bec5ef-fc02-458d-9b86-98132d9c168f/scratchpad/migrate_notices.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Tokenize-based migration of site_notices.append(...) / site_notices += builder(...)\nto the canonical sc.add_notice / sc.add_notices path.  Byte-safe: uses tokenize so parens\ninside f-strings are never miscounted.\"\"\"\nimport io\nimport sys\nimport tokenize\n\nPATH = \"/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails\"\n\nsrc = open(PATH).read()\nlines = src.splitlines(keepends=True)\n# absolute offset of the start of each 1-indexed line\nline_off = [0]\nfor ln in lines:\n    line_off.append(line_off[-1] + len(ln))\n\ndef off(pos):\n    row, col = pos\n    return line_off[row - 1] + col\n\ntoks = list(tokenize.generate_tokens(io.StringIO(src).readline))\n# keep only meaningful tokens for structural scanning (skip NL/NEWLINE/INDENT/COMMENT/etc.)\nsig = [t for t in toks if t.type not in (\n    tokenize.NL, tokenize.NEWLINE, tokenize.INDENT, tokenize.DEDENT,\n    tokenize.COMMENT, tokenize.ENCODING, tokenize.ENDMARKER)]\n\ndef match_close(start_i):\n    \"\"\"Given index of an OP '(' token in `sig`, return index of its matching ')'.\"\"\"\n    depth = 0\n    for j in range(start_i, len(sig)):\n        if sig[j].type == tokenize.OP and sig[j].string in \"([{\":\n            depth += 1\n        elif sig[j].type == tokenize.OP and sig[j].string in \")]}\":\n            depth -= 1\n            if depth == 0:\n                return j\n    raise RuntimeError(\"unbalanced\")\n\nedits = []  # (start_off, end_off, replacement)\ni = 0\nn_append = n_plus = 0\nwhile i < len(sig):\n    t = sig[i]\n    if t.type == tokenize.NAME and t.string == \"site_notices\":\n        # pattern A: site_notices . append ( ... )\n        if (i + 3 < len(sig) and sig[i+1].string == \".\" and sig[i+2].string == \"append\"\n                and sig[i+3].string == \"(\"):\n            open_i = i + 3\n            close_i = match_close(open_i)\n            # replace 'site_notices.append' text with 'sc.add_notice'\n            edits.append((off(t.start), off(sig[i+2].end), \"sc.add_notice\"))\n            # insert ', site_notices' before the matching ')'\n            edits.append((off(sig[close_i].start), off(sig[close_i].start), \", site_notices\"))\n            n_append += 1\n            i = close_i + 1\n            continue\n        # pattern B: site_notices += <call> ( ... )\n        if i + 1 < len(sig) and sig[i+1].string == \"+=\":\n            # RHS must be NAME '(' ... ')'\n            if not (sig[i+2].type == tokenize.NAME and sig[i+3].string == \"(\"):\n                raise RuntimeError(f\"unexpected += RHS near line {t.start[0]}: {sig[i+2].string!r}\")\n            open_i = i + 3\n            close_i = match_close(open_i)\n            # replace 'site_notices +=' with 'sc.add_notices('\n            edits.append((off(t.start), off(sig[i+1].end), \"sc.add_notices(\"))\n            # insert ', site_notices)' after the builder call's ')'\n            edits.append((off(sig[close_i].end), off(sig[close_i].end), \", site_notices)\"))\n            n_plus += 1\n            i = close_i + 1\n            continue\n    i += 1\n\n# apply edits from the end\nedits.sort(key=lambda e: e[0], reverse=True)\nout = src\nfor start, end, repl in edits:\n    out = out[:start] + repl + out[end:]\n\nopen(PATH, \"w\").write(out)\nprint(f\"append->add_notice: {n_append}   +=->add_notices: {n_plus}\")\n"
}
```

**Step 12 — P9**: reproduce and identify the actual `link-name` node. Let me read the render test to see how axe reports, then surface the flagged node:

### ⚙ Tool call: `Read`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/tests/render/test_render.py"
}
```

### ↳ Tool result

```
1	"""Render tier: load the report HTML in a headless browser and check it renders cleanly
2	(test-suite SPEC §7.6) for both the WordPress and Drupal reports.
3	
4	The report's images are attached by Content-ID (cid:), which a standalone browser can't
5	resolve, so we extract them from the .eml, write them locally, and rewrite the cid: refs
6	before loading.  Then we assert: the DOM structure is present, the banner image actually
7	resolves to pixels, there are no console errors, and axe-core (vendored locally — no network)
8	reports no serious/critical accessibility violations outside a small, explicit allowlist.
9	
10	If Chromium can't launch (browser binary or system libraries not installed), the test SKIPS
11	with the exact setup command rather than erroring.
12	"""
13	import email
14	import json
15	import re
16	from pathlib import Path
17	
18	import pytest
19	
20	pytestmark = pytest.mark.render
21	
22	_CID_REF = re.compile(r"cid:([^\"'\s>]+)")
23	_SETUP_HINT = "one-time setup: python -m playwright install --with-deps chromium"
24	_AXE = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent / "vendor" / "axe.min.js"
25	
26	# Accessibility rules we currently accept for this static, email-oriented HTML report.
27	# Keep this list SMALL and explicit so genuinely new serious/critical issues still fail.
28	#   * color-contrast: email palette is brand-fixed and out of scope for this tool.
29	#   * region: email HTML has no ARIA landmarks by design.
30	#   * link-name: PRE-EXISTING template defect (some links lack discernible text) — a real
31	#     WCAG issue tracked in development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md (P9),
32	#     allowlisted only so the smoke still catches NEW regressions; remove when the template
33	#     is fixed.
34	_AXE_ALLOWLIST = {"color-contrast", "region", "link-name"}
35	
36	
37	def _rewrite_cids_to_local(rendered, dest_dir):
38	    """Extract inline images from the .eml and rewrite the HTML's cid: refs to file URIs."""
39	    msg = email.message_from_bytes(rendered["eml"].read_bytes())
40	    cid_to_uri = {}
41	    for part in msg.walk():
42	        cid = part.get("Content-ID")
43	        if cid and part.get_content_maintype() == "image":
44	            key = cid.strip("<>")
45	            out = dest_dir / f"{key}.{part.get_content_subtype()}"
46	            out.write_bytes(part.get_payload(decode=True))
47	            cid_to_uri[key] = out.as_uri()
48	    html = rendered["html"].read_text()
49	    html = _CID_REF.sub(lambda m: cid_to_uri.get(m.group(1), m.group(0)), html)
50	    page_file = dest_dir / "render.html"
51	    page_file.write_text(html)
52	    return page_file
53	
54	
55	@pytest.mark.parametrize("report_fixture", ["rendered_report", "rendered_report_drupal"])
56	def test_report_renders_cleanly(report_fixture, request, tmp_path):
57	    from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
58	
59	    rendered = request.getfixturevalue(report_fixture)
60	    page_file = _rewrite_cids_to_local(rendered, tmp_path)
61	
62	    pw = sync_playwright().start()
63	    try:
64	        try:
65	            browser = pw.chromium.launch()
66	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - environment provisioning, not a test failure
67	            pytest.skip(f"Chromium can't launch ({type(exc).__name__}); {_SETUP_HINT}")
68	        try:
69	            page = browser.new_page()
70	            console_errors = []
71	            page.on("console", lambda m: console_errors.append(m.text) if m.type == "error" else None)
72	            page.goto(page_file.as_uri(), wait_until="load")
73	
74	            # ── structure ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
75	            assert "Pantheon Traffic Report" in page.title()
76	            assert page.locator("img.banner_image").count() == 1
77	            assert page.locator("img.chart_image").count() >= 1
78	            banner_width = page.eval_on_selector("img.banner_image", "el => el.naturalWidth")
79	            assert banner_width and banner_width > 0  # banner actually loaded
80	
81	            # ── no console errors (email HTML has no JS; broken assets would show here) ─
82	            assert console_errors == [], f"console errors: {console_errors}"
83	
84	            # ── accessibility smoke (axe-core, vendored; offline) ─────────────────────
85	            page.add_script_tag(path=str(_AXE))
86	            result = page.evaluate("async () => await axe.run(document)")
87	            serious = [
88	                v for v in result["violations"]
89	                if v.get("impact") in ("serious", "critical") and v["id"] not in _AXE_ALLOWLIST
90	            ]
91	            assert not serious, "axe serious/critical violations: " + json.dumps(
92	                [(v["id"], v["impact"]) for v in serious]
93	            )
94	        finally:
95	            browser.close()
96	    finally:
97	        pw.stop()
98
```

1	"""Integration tests for check/umich/sitelens.py (test-suite SPEC §7.4).

10	from importlib.machinery import SourceFileLoader
11	from pathlib import Path
12	
13	import pytest
14

18	PORTAL_ID = 101

22	@pytest.fixture
23	def sitelens(psh):
24	    path = Path(psh.__file__).parent / "check" / "umich" / "sitelens.py"
25	    loader = SourceFileLoader("umich_sitelens_probe", str(path))
26	    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_loader(loader.name, loader)
27	    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
28	    loader.exec_module(module)
29	    return module
30	
31	
32	def _score(a, p, bp, seo, cfg_id):
33	    return {
34	        "configuration_id": cfg_id,
35	        "accessibility_score": a,
36	        "performance_score": p,
37	        "best_practices_score": bp,
38	        "seo_score": seo,
39	        "timestamp": TS,
40	    }
41	
42	
43	def test_create_gauge_image_returns_png(sitelens):
44	    for value, color in [(95, sitelens.GOOD_SCORE_COLOR), (60, sitelens.OK_SCORE_COLOR), (10, sitelens.BAD_SCORE_COLOR)]:
45	        img = sitelens.create_gauge_image(value, color, "Test")
46	        assert isinstance(img, bytes)
47	        assert img[:8] == b"\x89PNG\r\n\x1a\n"  # PNG signature
48	
49	
50	def test_scores_section_and_attachments(sitelens, reset_sc):
51	    sc = reset_sc
52	    sc.config = {"UMich": {"portal": {"sites": {SITE: {"id": PORTAL_ID}}}}}
53	    sitelens.sitelens_configured_scans_by_site = {PORTAL_ID: [1, 2]}
54	    # Per-scan scores DIFFER, so the cross-scan averaging is genuinely exercised (a "use only the
55	    # first/last scan" bug would give different values and fail).  Means -> accessibility 90 (GOOD),
56	    # performance 70 (OK), best_practices 40 (BAD), seo 100 (GOOD).
57	    sitelens.sitelens_scores = {
58	        1: _score(0.80, 0.60, 0.30, 1.00, 1),
59	        2: _score(1.00, 0.80, 0.50, 1.00, 2),
60	    }
61	    ctx = {"site": {"name": SITE}, "attachments": [], "sections": []}
62	
63	    sitelens.check_sitelens_scores(ctx)
64	
65	    # One inline PNG attachment per score (4), each with a cid.
66	    assert len(ctx["attachments"]) == 4
67	    for att in ctx["attachments"]:
68	        assert att["maintype"] == "image" and att["subtype"] == "png"
69	        assert att["disposition"] == "inline"
70	        assert att["cid"] and att["data"][:8] == b"\x89PNG\r\n\x1a\n"
71	
72	    assert len(ctx["sections"]) == 1
73	    section = ctx["sections"][0]
74	    assert section["heading"] == "SiteLens"
75	    # Averaged scores appear in the plaintext, exercising each color band.
76	    for band in ("90 / 100", "70 / 100", "40 / 100", "100 / 100"):
77	        assert band in section["text"]
78	    # HTML references the inline images by cid.
79	    assert section["content"].count("cid:") == 4
80	
81	
82	def test_urls_notice_when_too_few_paths(sitelens, reset_sc):
83	    sc = reset_sc
84	    sc.config = {"UMich": {"portal": {"sites": {SITE: {"id": PORTAL_ID}}}}}

  "content": "# Configuring the report email sender and SMTP server\n\nThe monthly report emails' identity (who they appear to be from, who dry-run mail goes to,\nwhich server sends them) is controlled by two optional sections in your\n`pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` config file: `[Email]` and `[SMTP]`.\n\n**Every key below is optional.** If you omit a key — or omit the whole section — the tool\nfalls back to the University of Michigan defaults it originally shipped with. If you run the\ntool for a different institution, set these so your reports come from *your* addresses.\n\n## `[Email]` — sender identity and addressing\n\n```toml\n[Email]\nfrom        = \"Example Web Team <webteam@example.edu>\"   # the From: header\nreply_to    = \"webteam@example.edu\"                       # the Reply-to: header\nmsgid_domain = \"reports.example.edu\"                      # domain used in inline-image IDs\n\n# Sent only on a real run (with --for-real):\nbcc         = \"ops@example.edu\"                            # the Bcc: header\n\n# Dry-run addressing. These two keys control that dry-run To: line:\ndry_run_to             = \"ops@example.edu\"                # an extra fixed dry-run recipient\ndry_run_username_domain = \"example.edu\"                   # {smtp-username}@<this> is added too\n```\n\n| Key | Controls | Default (U-M) |\n|-----|----------|---------------|\n| `from` | `From:` header | `University of Michigan Webmaster Team <webmaster@umich.edu>` |\n| `reply_to` | `Reply-to:` header | `webmaster@umich.edu` |\n| `bcc` | `Bcc:` header (only with `--for-real`) | `januside@go.mail.umich.edu, its-webmaster@go.mail.umich.edu` |\n| `dry_run_to` | fixed recipient on a dry run | `januside@go.mail.umich.edu` |\n| `dry_run_username_domain` | domain appended to `--smtp-username` on a dry run | `umich.edu` |\n| `msgid_domain` | domain in the inline images' `Content-ID` | `webservices.umich.edu` |\n\n## `[SMTP]` — outgoing mail server\n\n```toml\n[SMTP]\nhost = \"smtp.example.edu\"\nport = 465\n```\n\n| Key | Controls | Default (U-M) |\n|-----|----------|---------------|\n| `host` | SMTP server hostname | `smtp.mail.umich.edu` |\n| `port` | SMTP server port (SSL) | `465` |\n\nThe SMTP **password** is never stored in the config file — it is read from the\n`SMTP_PASSWORD` environment variable at send time, and the username comes from the\n`--smtp-username` command-line option.\n\n## Safety reminder\n\nWithout `--for-real`, the tool sends **all** mail to the logged-in user (the dry-run\naddressing above), never to site owners. Note existing notice dicts carry their own bespoke\n  `text`, so `add_notice`'s defaults are no-ops for them. Call sites that index into the result use `terminus_data(...)`, which raises\n  the named `TerminusError` when the command was fatal or returned no data (org-level calls\n  abort; per-site calls skip that site). `wp()`/`wp_eval()` and `drush()`/`drush_php_script()`\n  run WordPress and Drupal commands on a `site.env` remotely (all return 3-tuples too);\n  `wp_error()`/`drush_error()` build alert notices from command failures. 174	- **Safety interlock.** `run_program()` in conftest is the only sanctioned way to run the program
175	  in a subprocess; it raises `ForbiddenFlagError` if `--all`/`-a`/`--for-real` appear, and
176	  `ForbiddenLiveDataError` if `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` would run live or against

178	  default DB is also sqlite). Never bypass it. Tests use only `its-wws-test1`/`its-wws-test2`,
179	  read-only.
180	- **Pure-helper seam.** Four pure functions were extracted from `main()` as module-level defs so
181	  they're importable as `psh.<fn>` and unit/property tested: `overage_blocks`, `contract_year_end`,
182	  `estimate_month_visits`, and `plan_costs` (the cost model — DB-free via an injected
183	  `op_lookup(month)`; the U-M downgrade guardrails/notices remain inline in `main()` for the later
184	  de-monolith stage). The extraction is behavior-preserving (WordPress golden byte-identical).
185	- **Offline e2e determinism.** The shim-backed run uses `tests/fixtures/config/minimal.toml`,
186	  seeded traffic, `--date 2026-03-31` (a mid-year date avoids the U-M contract-year-end path),
187	  and a `domain:list` fixture reduced to the platform domain (so no live DNS). Golden snapshots
188	  normalize the volatile `make_msgid` CIDs; refresh with `./run-tests --update-goldens`. There are
189	  two goldens: WordPress (`its-wws-test1`, fixtures in `tests/fixtures/terminus/`) and Drupal
190	  (`its-wws-test2`, `tests/fixtures/terminus-drupal/`, selected via `run_program(fixtures_dir=…)`).
191	  Refresh WordPress fixtures with `./run-tests --record`, Drupal with `python tests/tools/record.py
192	  --drupal` (both trim the org list to the one test site and scrub team emails).
193	- **The offline golden only reaches the ≤4-month "not enough data" state** (its recorded metrics
194	  fall after the March report date), so the extracted `plan_costs` cost model is exercised
195	  end-to-end by `tests/e2e/test_recommendation_e2e.py` (seeds >4 in-window months) plus its
196	  unit/property tests — not by the golden. The render tier vendors axe-core locally
197	  (`tests/vendor/axe.min.js`) so it stays offline.
198	- **The reusable (non-UMich) path had latent bugs** that production never hit because U-M always
199	  runs with the UMich plugin enabled. Several U-M-specific code paths in the core script are not
200	  yet behind the `[UMich].enabled` flag; the planned refactor should move them out. When adding
201	  code, keep institution-specific logic behind config flags / the `umich` plugin+check packages.
202
```

## Summary

All ten problems from `PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` are resolved per the approved, twice-adversarially-reviewed SPEC (`development/2026-07-05-fix-existing-problems/SPEC.md`).

| # | Outcome |
|---|---------|
| **P1** | No change — already correct (existing e2e pins the ≤4-month state). |
| **P2** | `load_news_items()` extracted; config-inline `[News.<x>]` items now added (also fixed a latent `KeyError` when `[News]` is absent). |
| **P3** | `terminus()` returns `(result, errors, fatal)`; `terminus_data()` raises the named `TerminusError`; all 10 call sites updated (org-level abort, per-site skip). |
| **P4** | `classify_hostname_dns()` separates transient (Timeout/NoNameservers) from definitive failures; transient ones get a distinct warning notice and no longer masquerade as "not in DNS". |
| **P5** | Deferred (documented) — behind `--all` + disabled SMTP. |
| **P6** | Wrapper annotations/docstrings corrected to the real 3-tuple. |
| **P7** | Comment now references `sc.options.all`. |
| **P8** | Pragmatic subset: email/SMTP → `[Email]`/`[SMTP]` config (byte-identical U-M defaults); fqdns-gated Cloudflare checks behind `umich_enabled()`. |
| **P9** | Root cause was the caption's `<a href="{{site_url}}">` rendering `<a href=""></a>` when blank — now guarded; `link-name` removed from the axe allowlist and enforced. |
| **P10** | `build_plan_over_time()` + empty-`plan_on_day` guard render a clean "no traffic yet" outcome instead of `IndexError`. |

Plus the accepted expansions: **`sc.add_notice()` is now canonical** (25 appends + 4 builders migrated, byte-identical) and a **third non-U-M golden** proves the P8 config path.

- `./run-tests --fast` → **171 passed, 1 skipped** (pre-existing SMTP skip).
- `./run-tests` (all tiers incl. `live`) → **173 passed, 1 skipped**.

One note for a future session, recorded in CLAUDE.md and the SPEC: the full relocation of the fqdns-gated checks into the `umich` package still needs a new post-gather per-site hook seam (the existing `check` hook fires before the plugin/DNS data exists), and the template still hardcodes some U-M branding — both intentionally deferred out of P8's pragmatic subset.

## User

Move the definition of `site_context` as far up in the site for loop as possible, make it an instance of a site_context class, replace all instances of `site_notices` in that loop with `site_context['notices']`, and make the `add_notice` and `add_notices` functions methods on the `site_context` class.  Interview me about any gaps or contradictions in these requirements.  If there is a better solution, push back on my proposal.

## Assistant

I've mapped the current state. Your proposal is sound and I'd implement it, but there are three genuine gaps/contradictions to resolve first, plus one place I'd push back.

**What I found in the current code:**
- `site_notices = []` at loop top (L1221); `site_context` dict is built later (L1465) with `"notices": site_notices` (same list object) plus `site`/`sections`/`attachments`. The check hook runs right after (L1471).
- 56 `site_notices` references and 46 `sc.add_notice`/`sc.add_notices` call sites in the loop; one external caller in `check/umich/sitelens.py`.

**Contradictions/gaps in the requirements:**

1. **"a class" + "`site_context['notices']`" (subscript) are only compatible if it's a `dict` subclass** (or implements `__getitem__`). A "proper" attribute class would mean `site_context.notices`, and would force rewriting *all* the other `site_context['sections']`/`['attachments']`/`['site']` accesses too — much larger churn.
2. **"methods" vs "replace `site_notices` with `site_context['notices']`" collide at the add-sites.** If `add_notice` is a method, the 46 add-sites become `site_context.add_notice(dict)` — *not* `sc.add_notice(dict, site_context['notices'])`. So the subscript form only applies to the ~4 *read* sites (`for n in site_notices`, `sorted_notices = [...]`, the not-in-dns aggregation). I'll implement it that way unless you disagree.
3. **The methods currently live in `script_context.py` (`sc`) and are used by the `umich` package.** Making them methods orphans `sc.add_notice`/`sc.add_notices`.

**Where I'd push back:** a `dict` subclass that also grows `add_notice` behavior trends toward a "god object." A cleaner OO alternative is leaving `site_context` a plain dict and giving `notices` its own small collection type with `.add()`. But that diverges from your request and adds a type for little gain — I think the `dict`-subclass `SiteContext` is the right-sized fit. Byte-identical goldens remain the hard constraint either way.

## Assistant

Now I have everything mapped. The plan:
- **script_context.py**: replace the `add_notice`/`add_notices` free functions with `class SiteContext(dict)` (methods `add_notice`, `add_notices`, `add_section`, `add_attachment`).
- **core script**: remove `site_notices = []` (L1221), construct `site_context = sc.SiteContext(site)` after the Sandbox skip (L1277), remove the old dict construction (L1465); then a tokenize transform converts `sc.add_notice(…, site_notices)` → `site_context.add_notice(…)` and bare `site_notices` reads → `site_context['notices']`.
- **sitelens.py + tests**: switch to the methods / construct `SiteContext`.

Starting with the class:
